sīreṇa sahitau pārtha dhānyaṃ droṇakasaṃkhyayā
alaṃkṛtāṃ savatsāṃ ca kṣīriṇīṃ taruṇīṃ sitām
raktāṃ vā kṛṣṇavarṇāṃ vā pāṭalāṃ kapilāṃ tathā
kāṃsyadohanasaṃyuktāṃ rukmakhuravibhūṣaṇām
svarṇaśṛṅgīṃ savatsāṃ ca brāhmaṇāyopapādayet
prīyatāṃ me jagannāthā harakṛṣṇapitāmahāḥ
saṃsārarakṣaṇī devī surabhī māṃ samuddharet
putrārthaṃ yāḥ striyaḥ pārtha hyeraṇḍīsaṅgame nṛpa
snāpyante rudrasūktaiśca caturvedodbhavaistathā
caturbhirbrāhmaṇaiḥ śastaṃ dvābhyāṃ yogyaiśca kārayet
ekena sārdrakumbhena dāmpatyamabhiṣecayet
daivajñenaiva caikena athavā sāmagena vā
pañcaratnasamāyuktaṃ kumbhe tatraiva kārayet
gandhatoyasamāyuktaṃ sarvauṣadhivimiśritam
āmrapallavasaṃyuktam aśvatthamadhukaṃ tathā
guṇṭhitaṃ sitavastreṇa sitacandanacarcitam
sitapuṣpaistu saṃchannaṃ siddhārthakṛtamadhyamam
kāṃsyapātre tu saṃsthāpya putrārthī deśikottamaḥ
aṅgalagnaṃ tu yadvastraṃ kaṭakābharaṇaṃ tathā
tatsarvaṃ maṇḍale tyājyaṃ siddhyarthaṃ cātmanastadā
praṇamya bhāskaraṃ paścādācāryaṃ rudrarūpiṇam
madhuraṃ ca tato 'śnīyād devyā bhuvana uttame
phaladānaṃ ca viprāya chatraṃ tāmbūlameva ca
upānahau ca yānaṃ ca sa bhaved duḥkhavarjitaḥ
bhāskare krīḍate loke yāvad ābhūtasamplavam
dānaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ sarvaṃ śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham
yathā nadīnadāḥ sarve sāgare yānti saṃkṣayam
evaṃ pāpāni naśyanti hyeraṇḍīsaṅgame nṛṇām
samantācchastrapātena hyeraṇḍīsaṅgame nṛpa
bhrūṇahatyāsamaṃ pāpaṃ naśyate śaṅkaro 'bravīt
prāṇatyāgaṃ ca yo bhaktyā jātavedasi kārayet
anāśakaṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha jale vā tadanantaram
pañcasāhasrikaṃ mānaṃ varṣāṇāṃ jātavedasi
jale trīṇi sahasrāṇyanāśake ṣaṣṭiṃ bhuñjate
kākā bakāḥ kapotāśca hyulūkāḥ paśavas tathā
saṃgamodakasaṃspṛṣṭās te yānti paramāṃ gatim
vṛkṣāśca tatpadaṃ jñātvā yāṃ gatiṃ yānti yoginaḥ
eraṇḍikā mayā devī dṛṣṭo me manmatheśvaraḥ
kiṃ samartho yamo ruṣṭo bhadro bhadrāṇi paśyati
mṛttikāṃ saṅgamodbhūtāṃ ye ca guṇṭhanti nityaśaḥ
bhrūṇahatyādipāpāni naśyante nātra saṃśayaḥ
eraṇḍīsaṅgame martyo luṇṭhyamāno narādhipa
sarvapāpairvinirmuktaḥ padaṃ gacchatyanāmayam
eraṇḍyāḥ saṅgamaṃ martyāḥ kīrtayantyāśramasthitāḥ
vimuktapāpā jāyante satyaṃ śaṅkarabhāṣitam
eraṇḍīpādapāgraistu dṛṣṭaiḥ pāpaṃ vyapohati
tīrthākhyānamidaṃ puṇyaṃ ye paṭhiṣyanti mānavāḥ
śṛṇvanti cāpare bhaktyā muktapāpā bhavanti te
etatte sarvamākhyātam eraṇḍīsaṅgamaṃ nṛpa
bhūyaścānyat pravakṣyāmi sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe eraṇḍīsaṅgamatīrthaphalamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma tryadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahīpālaṃ sauvarṇaśilamuttamam
prakhyātamuttare kūle sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram
samantācchatapātena munisaṅghaiḥ purā kṛtam
revāyāṃ durlabhaṃ sthānaṃ saṅgamasya samīpataḥ
vibhaktaṃ hastamātraṃ ca puṇyakṣetraṃ narādhipa
suvarṇaśilake snātvā pūjayitvā maheśvaram
natvā tu bhāskaraṃ devaṃ hotavyaṃ ca hutāśane
bilvenājyavimiśreṇa bilvapatrairathāpi vā
prīyatāṃ me jagannātho vyādhir naśyatu me dhruvam
dvijāya kāñcane datte yatphalaṃ tacchṛṇuṣva me
bahusvarṇasya yatproktaṃ yāgasya phalamuttamam
tathāsau labhate sarvaṃ kāñcanaṃ yaḥ prayacchati
tena dānena pūtātmā mṛtaḥ svargamavāpnuyāt
rudrasyānucaras tāvad yāvad indrāścaturdaśa
tataḥ svargāvatīrṇastu jāyate viśade kule
dhanadhānyasamopetaḥ punaḥ smarati tajjalam
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe suvarṇaśilātīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma caturadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
karañjākhyaṃ tato gacchet sopavāso jitendriyaḥ
tatra snātvā tu rājendra sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
arcayitvā mahādevaṃ dattvā dānaṃ tu bhaktitaḥ
suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ vāpi maṇimauktikavidrumān
pādukopānahau chatraṃ śayyāṃ prāvaraṇāni ca
koṭikoṭiguṇaṃ sarvaṃ jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe karañjatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma pañcādhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahīpāla tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam
saubhāgyakaraṇaṃ divyaṃ naranārīmanoramam
tatra yā durbhagā nārī naro vā nṛpasattama
snātvārcayed umārudrau saubhāgyaṃ tasya jāyate
tṛtīyāyāmahorātraṃ sopavāso jitendriyaḥ
nimantrayed dvijaṃ bhaktyā sapatnīkaṃ surūpiṇam
gandhamālyairalaṃkṛtya vastradhūpādivāsitam
bhojayet pāyasānnena kṛsareṇātha bhaktitaḥ
bhojayitvā yathānyāyaṃ pradakṣiṇamudāharet
prīyatāṃ me mahādevaḥ sapatnīko vṛṣadhvajaḥ
yathā te devadeveśa na viyogaḥ kadācana
mamāpi karuṇāṃ kṛtvā tathāstviti vicintayet
evaṃ kṛte tatastasya yatpuṇyaṃ samudāhṛtam
tatte sarvaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathā devena bhāṣitam
daurbhāgyaṃ durgatiścaiva dāridryaṃ śokabandhanam
vandhyatvaṃ saptajanmāni jāyate na yudhiṣṭhira
jyeṣṭhamāse site pakṣe tṛtīyāyāṃ viśeṣataḥ
tatra gatvā tu yo bhaktyā pañcāgniṃ sādhayettataḥ
so 'pi pāpairaśeṣaistu mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
guggulaṃ dahate yastu dvidhā cittavivarjitaḥ
śarīraṃ bhedayed yastu gauryāścaiva samīpataḥ
tasminkarmapraviṣṭasya utkrāntir jāyate yadi
dehapāte vrajet svargam ityevaṃ śaṅkaro 'bravīt
sitaraktaistathā pītairvastraiśca vividhaiḥ śubhaiḥ
brāhmaṇīṃ brāhmaṇaṃ caiva pūjayitvā yathāvidhi
puṣpairnānāvidhaiścaiva gandhadhūpaiḥ suśobhanaiḥ
kaṇṭhasūtrakasindūraiḥ kuṅkumena vilepayet
kalpayeta striyaṃ gaurīṃ brāhmaṇaṃ śivarūpiṇam
teṣāṃ tadrūpakaṃ kṛtvā dānamutsṛjyate tataḥ
kaṅkaṇaṃ karṇaveṣṭaṃ ca kaṇṭhikāṃ mudrikāṃ tathā
saptadhānyaṃ tathā caiva bhojanaṃ nṛpasattama
anyānyapi ca dānāni tasmiṃstīrthe dadāti yaḥ
sarvadānaiśca yatpuṇyaṃ prāpnuyānnātra saṃśayaḥ
sahasraguṇitaṃ sarvaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
śaṅkareṇa samaṃ tasmādbhogaṃ bhuṅkte hyanuttamam
saubhāgyaṃ tasya vipulaṃ jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
aputro labhate putramadhano dhanamāpnuyāt
rājendra kāmadaṃ tīrthaṃ narmadāyāṃ vyavasthitam
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe kāmadatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaḍuttaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gaccheta rājendra bhaṇḍārītīrtham uttamam
daridracchedakaraṇaṃ yugānyekonaviṃśatiḥ
dhanadena tapastaptvā prasanne padmasambhave
tatraiva svalpadānena prāptaṃ vittasya rakṣaṇam
tatra gatvā tu yo bhaktyā snātvā vittaṃ prayacchati
tasya vittaparicchedo na kadācid bhaviṣyati
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe bhaṇḍārītīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma saptottaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahīpāla rohiṇītīrthamuttamam
vikhyātaṃ triṣu lokeṣu sarvapāpaharaṃ param
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
rohiṇītīrthamāhātmyaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam
śrotumicchāmi tattvena tanme tvaṃ vaktumarhasi
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tasminnekārṇave ghore naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame
udadhau ca śayānasya devadevasya cakriṇaḥ
nābhau samutthitaṃ padmaṃ ravimaṇḍalasannibham
karṇikākesaropetaṃ patraiśca samalaṃkṛtam
tatra brahmā samutpannaścaturvadanapaṅkajaḥ
kiṃ karomīti deveśa ājñā me dīyatāṃ prabho
evamuktastu deveśaḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ
uvāca madhurāṃ vāṇīṃ tadā devaṃ pitāmaham
sarasvatyāṃ mahābāho lokaṃ kuru mamājñayā
bhūtagrāmamaśeṣasya utpādanavidhikṣayam
etacchrutaṃ tu vacanaṃ padmanābhasya bhārata
cintayāmāsa bhagavānsaptarṣīnhitakāmyayā
kramātte cintitāḥ prājñāḥ pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ
prācetaso vasiṣṭhaśca bhṛgurnārada eva ca
yajñe prācetaso dakṣo mahātejāḥ prajāpatiḥ
dakṣasyāpi tathā jātāḥ pañcāśadduhitaro 'nagha
dadau sa daśa dharmāya kaśyapāya trayodaśa
tathaiva sa mahābhāgaḥ saptaviṃśatimindave
rohiṇīnāma yā tāsāṃ madhye tasya narādhipa
aniṣṭā sarvanārīṇāṃ bhartuścaiva viśeṣataḥ
tataḥ sā paramaṃ kṛtvā vairāgyaṃ nṛpasattama
āgatya narmadātīre cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ
ekarātrais trirātraiśca ṣaḍdvādaśabhireva ca
pakṣamāsopavāsaiśca karśayanti kalevaram
ārādhayantī satataṃ mahiṣāsuranāśinīṃ
devīṃ bhagavatīṃ tāta sarvārtivinivāraṇīm
snātvā snātvā jale nityaṃ narmadāyāḥ śucismitā
tatastuṣṭā mahābhāgā devī nārāyaṇī nṛpa
prasannā te mahābhāge vratena niyamena ca
etacchrutvā tu vacanaṃ rohiṇī śaśinaḥ priyā
yathā bhavāmi na cirāttathā bhavatu mānade
evamastviti sā coktvā bhavānī bhaktavatsalā
stūyamānā munigaṇaistatraivāntaradhīyata
tadāprabhṛti tattīrthaṃ rohiṇī śaśinaḥ priyā
saṃjātā sarvakālaṃ tu vallabhā nṛpasattama
tatra tīrthe tu yā nārī naro vā snāni bhaktitaḥ
vallabhā jāyate sā tu bhartur vai rohiṇī yathā
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ kaścitprāṇatyāgaṃ karoti vai
saptajanmāni dāmpatyaviyogo na bhavet kvacit
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe rohiṇīsomanāthatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭottaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahīpāla cakratīrthamanuttamam
senāpuramitikhyātaṃ sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram
saināpatyābhiṣekāya devadevena cakriṇā
ānītaśca mahāseno devaiḥ sendrapurogamaiḥ
dānavānāṃ vadhārthāya jayāya ca divaukasām
bhūmidānena viprendrāṃs tarpayitvā yathāvidhi
śaṅkhabherīninādaiśca paṭahānāṃ ca nisvanaiḥ
vīṇāveṇumṛdaṅgaiśca jhallarīsvaramaṅgalaiḥ
tataḥ kṛtvā svanaṃ ghoraṃ dānavo baladarpitaḥ
rururnāma vighātārthamabhiṣekasya cāgataḥ
hastyaśvarathapattyoghaiḥ pūrayanvai diśo daśa
tatra tena mahadyuddhaṃ pravṛttaṃ kila bhārata
śaktyṛṣṭipāśamuśalaiḥ khaḍgaistomaraṭaṅkanaiḥ
bhallaiḥ karṇikanārācaiḥ kabandhapaṭasaṃkulaiḥ
tatastu tāṃ śatrubalasya senāṃ kṣaṇena cāpancyutabāṇaghātaiḥ
vidhvastahastyaśvarathānmahātmā jagrāha cakraṃ ripusaṅghanāśanaḥ
jvalacca cakraṃ niśitaṃ bhayaṃkaraṃ surāsurāṇāṃ ca sudarśanaṃ raṇe
cakarta daityasya śirastadānīṃ karātpramuktaṃ madhughātinaśca tat
taṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasā vighnamabhiṣeke ṣaḍānanaḥ
tyaktvā tu tatra saṃsthānaṃ cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ
muktaṃ cakraṃ vināśāya hariṇā lokadhāriṇā
dvidalaṃ dānavaṃ kṛtvā papāta vimale jale
tadā prabhṛti tattīrthaṃ cakratīrthamiti śrutam
sarvapāpavināśāya nirmitaṃ viśvamūrtinā
cakratīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayed devamacyutam
puṇḍarīkasya yajñasya phalamāpnoti mānavaḥ
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayed brāhmaṇāñchubhān
śāntadāntajitakrodhānsa labhetkoṭijaṃ phalam
tatra tīrthe tu yo bhaktyā tyajate dehamātmanaḥ
viṣṇulokaṃ mṛto yāti jayaśabdādimaṅgalaiḥ
krīḍayitvā yathākāmaṃ devagandharvapūjitaḥ
ihāgatya ca bhūyo 'pi jāyate vipule kule

kathitaṃ te mahābhāga bhūyaścānyacchṛṇuṣva me
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe senāpure cakratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma navottaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
dhautapāpaṃ tato gacchen mahāpātakanāśanam
samīpe cakratīrthasya viṣṇunā nirmitaṃ purā
nihatair dānavair ghorair devadevo janārdanaḥ
tatpāpasya vināśārthaṃ dānavāntodbhavasya ca
tatra tīrthe jitakrodhaścacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ
duścaraṃ maunamāsthāya hyaśakyaṃ devadānavaiḥ
snātvā dattvā dvijātibhyo dānāni vividhāni ca
tatkṣaṇāt supāpas tu gatastadvaiṣṇavaṃ padam
evaṃ yuktastu yastatra pāpaṃ kṛtvā sudāruṇam
snātvā japtvā vidhānena mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe dhautapāpatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma daśottaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
narmadādakṣiṇe kūle tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam
skandena nirmitaṃ pūrvaṃ tapaḥ kṛtvā sudāruṇam
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
skandasya caritaṃ sarvamājanma dvijasattama
tīrthasya ca vidhiṃ puṇyaṃ kathayasva yathārthataḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
devadevena vai taptaṃ tapaḥ pūrvaṃ yudhiṣṭhira
vijñaptena suraiḥ sarvairumādevī vivāhitā
nāsti senāpatiḥ kaściddevānāṃ surasattama
nīyante dānavairghoraiḥ sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ
yathā niśā vinā candraṃ divaso bhāskaraṃ vinā
na śobhate muhūrtaṃ vai tathā senā vināyakā
evaṃ jñātvā mahādeva parayā dayayā vibho
senānīr dīyatāṃ kaścittriṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ
etacchrutvā śubhaṃ vākyaṃ devānāṃ parameśvaraḥ
kāmayāna umāṃ devīṃ sasmāra manasā smaram
tena mūrchitasarvāṅgaḥ kāmarūpo jagadguruḥ
kāmayāmāsa rudrāṇīṃ divyaṃ varṣaśataṃ kila
devarājastato jñātvā mahāmaithunagaṃ haram
saṃmantrya daivataiḥ sārddhaṃ praiṣayajjātavedasam
tena gatvā mahādevaḥ paramānandasaṃsthitaḥ
sahasā tena dṛṣṭo 'sau hāhetyuktvā samutthitaḥ
tataḥ kruddhā mahādevī śāpavācamuvāca ha
vepamānā mahārāja śṛṇu yatte vadāmyaham
ahaṃ yasmāt suraiḥ sarvairyācitā putrajanmani
kṛtā ratiśca viphalā saṃpreṣya jātavedasam
tasmātsarve putrahīnā bhaviṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ
hareṇoktastato vahnirasmākaṃ bījamāvaha
yathā bhavati lokeṣu tathā tvaṃ kartum arhasi
mama tejastvayā śakyaṃ gṛhītuṃ surasattama
devakāryārthasiddhyarthaṃ nānyaḥ śakto jagattraye
agniruvāca
tejasastava me deva kā śaktirdhāraṇe vibho
karoti bhasmasātsarvaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram
īśvara uvāca
udarasthena bījena yadi te jāyate rujā
tadā kṣipasva tattejo gaṅgātoye hutāśana
evamuktvā mahādevo 'moghaṃ bījamuttamam
havyavāhamukhe sarvaṃ prakṣipyāntaradhīyata
gate cādarśanaṃ deve dahyamāno hutāśanaḥ
gaṅgātoye vinikṣipya jagāma svaṃniveśanam
asahantī tu tattejo gaṅgāpi saritāṃ varā
śarastambe vinikṣipya jagāmāśu yathāgatam
tatra jātaṃ tu taddṛṣṭvā sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ
kṛttikāṃ preṣayāmāsuḥ stanyaṃ pāyayituṃ tadā
dṛṣṭvā tā āgatāḥ sarvā gaṅgāgarbhe mahāmateḥ
ṣaṇmukhaiḥ ṣaṇmukho bhūtvā pipāsurapibatstanam
jātakarmādisaṃskārānvedoktānpadmasambhavaḥ
cakāra sarvāndājendra vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā
ṣaṇmukhātṣaṇmukho nāma kārttikeyastu kṛttikāt
kumāraśca kumāratvād gaṅgāgarbho 'gnijo 'paraḥ
evaṃ kumāraḥ sambhūto hy anadhītya sa vedavit
śāstrāṇyanekāni veda cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ
devāraṇyeṣu sarveṣu nadīṣu ca nadeṣu ca
pṛthivyāṃ yāni tīrthāni samudrād yāni bhārata
tataḥ paryāyayogena narmadātaṭamāśritaḥ
narmadādakṣiṇe kūle cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ
ṛgyajuḥsāmavihitaṃ japañjāpyamaharniśam

tato varṣasahasrānte pūrṇe devo maheśvaraḥ
umayā sahitaḥ kāle tadā vacanam abravīt
īśvara uvāca
ahaṃ te varadastāta gaurī mātā pitā hyaham
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva yacceṣṭaṃ triṣu lokeṣu durlabham
ṣaṇmukha uvāca
yadi tuṣṭo mahādeva umayā saha śaṅkara
vṛṇomi mātāpitarau nānyā gatirmatirmama
etacchrutvā śubhaṃ vākyaṃ putrasya vadanāccyutam
tathetyuktvā tu snehena premṇā taṃ pariṣasvaje
tatastaṃ mūrdhnyupāghrāya hyumayovāca śaṅkaraḥ
īśvara uvāca
akṣayaścāvyayaścaiva senānīs tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi
śikhī ca te vāhanaṃ divyarūpo datto mayā śaktidharasya saṃkhye
surāsurādīṃśca jayeti coktvā jagāma kailāsavaraṃ mahātmā
gate cādarśanaṃ deve tadā sa śikhivāhanaḥ
sthāpayitvā mahādevaṃ jagāma surasannidhau
tadāprabhṛti tattīrthaṃ skandatīrthamiti śrutam
sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ martyānāṃ bhuvi durlabham
tatra tīrthe tu yo rājanbhaktyā snātvārcayecchivam
gandhamālyābhiṣekaiśca yājñikaṃ sa labhet phalam
skandatīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayet pitṛdevatāḥ

śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchettu rājendra tīrthamāṅgirasasya tu
uttare narmadākūle sarvapāpavināśanam

putrahetor yugasyādau cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ
nityaṃ triṣavaṇasnāyī japandevaṃ sanātanam
pūjayaṃśca mahādevaṃ kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādibhiḥ
dvādaśābde tataḥ pūrṇe tutoṣa parameśvaraḥ
vareṇa chandayāmāsa dvijam āṅgirasaṃ varam
vavre sa tu mahādevaṃ putraṃ putravatāṃ varam
vedavidyāvratasnātaṃ sarvaśāstraviśāradam
devānāṃ mantriṇaṃ rājan sarvalokeṣu pūjitam
brahmalakṣmyāḥ sadāvāsam akṣayaṃ cāvyayaṃ sutam

bhaviṣyati na sandehaścaivamuktvā yayau haraḥ

śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahārāja tīrtham aṅgārakaṃ param

śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchettu rājendra tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam
indratīrthetivikhyātaṃ narmadādakṣiṇe taṭe

kathayāmāsa tadvattamitihāsaṃ purātanam
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
viśvāsayitvā suciraṃ dharmaśatruṃ mahābalam
vṛtraṃ jitvātha hatvā tu gacchamānaṃ śacīpatim
niṣkrāmamāṇaṃ mārgeṇa brahmahatyā durāsadā
ahorātramaviśrāntā jagāma bhuvanatrayam
yatoyato brahmahaṇaṃ yāti yānena śobhanam
diśo bhāgaṃ suraiḥ sārddhaṃ tato hatyā na muñcati
brahmahatyā surāpānaṃ steyaṃ gurvaganāgamaḥ
pātakānāṃ gatirdṛṣṭā na tu viśvāsaghātinām
pāpakarmamukhaṃ dṛṣṭvā snānadānairviśudhyati
nārī vā puruṣo vāpi naiva viśvāsaghātinaḥ
evamādīni cānyāni śrutvā vākyāni devarāṭ
vacanaṃ tadvidhairuktaṃ viṣādamagamatparam
tyaktvā rājyaṃ suraiḥ sārdhaṃ jagāma tapa uttamam
putradāragṛhaṃ rājyaṃ vasūni vividhāni ca
phalānyetāni dharmasya śobhayanti janeśvaram
phalaṃ dharmasya bhuñjeti suhṛtsvajanabāndhavāḥ
paśyatāṃ sarvam eteṣāṃ pāpamekena bhujyate
paraṃ hi sukhamutsṛjya karśayanvai kalevaram
devarājo jagāmāsau tīrthānyāyatanāni ca
gaṅgātīrtheṣu sarveṣu yāmuneṣu tathaiva ca
sārasvateṣu sarveṣu sāmudreṣu pṛthakpṛthak
nadīṣu devakhāteṣu taḍāgeṣu saraḥsu ca
pāpaṃ na muñcate sarve paścāddevasamāgame
revāprabhavatīrtheṣu kūlayor ubhayor api
pūjayanvai mahādevaṃ skandatīrthaṃ samāsadat
tava sthitvopavāsaiśca kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādibhiḥ
karśayanvai svakaṃ dehaṃ na lebhe śarma vai kvacit
grīṣme pañcāgnimadhyastho varṣāsu sthaṇḍileśayaḥ
ārdravāsāstu hemante cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ
evaṃ tu tapatastasya indrasya viditātmanaḥ
vatsarāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi gatāni daśa bhārata
tatastvekādaśe prāpte varṣe tu nṛpasattama
sahasā bhagavāndevastu tutoṣa parameśvaraḥ
tathā brahmarṣayaḥ siddhā brahmaviṣṇupurogamāḥ
tatrājagmuḥ surāḥ sarve yatra devaḥ śatakratuḥ
dṛṣṭvā samāgatān devān ṛṣīṃścaiva mahāmatiḥ
uvāca praṇato bhūtvā sarvadevapurohitaḥ
viditaṃ sarvameteṣāṃ yathā vṛtravadhaḥ kṛtaḥ
yuṣmākaṃ cājñayā pūrvaṃ brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ
tathāpyevaṃ brahmahaṇaṃ matvā pāpasya kāriṇam
bhramantaṃ sarvatīrtheṣu brahmahatyā na muñcati
na nandati jagatsarvaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram
yathā vihīnacandrārkaṃ tathā rājyamanāyakam
tasmātsarve suraśreṣṭhā vijñāpyaṃ mama samprati
kurvantu śakraṃ nirdoṣaṃ tathā sarve maharṣayaḥ
bṛhaspatimukhodgīrṇaṃ śrutvā tadvacanaṃ śubham
tataḥ provāca bhagavānbrahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
etatpāpaṃ mahāghoraṃ brahmahatyāsamudbhavam
daivatebhyo 'tha bhūtebhyaścaturbhāgaṃ kṣipāmyaham
evaṃ muktvā kṣipaccaino jalopari mahāmatiḥ
avagāhya tataḥ peyā āpo vai nānyathā budhaiḥ
dharāyāmakṣipadbhāgaṃ dvitīyaṃ padmasaṃbhavaḥ
abhakṣyā tena saṃjātā sadākālaṃ vasuṃdharā
tadārdhamarddhaṃ nārīṇāṃ dvitīye 'hni yudhiṣṭhira
nikṣipya bhagavāndevaḥ punaranyajjagāda ha
asaṃgrāhyā tvasaṃgrāhyā tena jātā rajasvalā
caturdināni sā prājñaiḥ pāpasya mahato mahāt
caturthaṃ tu tato bhāgaṃ vibhajya parameśvaraḥ
kṛṣigorakṣyavāṇijyaiḥ śūdrasevākare dvije
tato 'bhinandayāmāsuḥ sarve devā maharṣayaḥ
devendraṃ vāgbhir iṣṭābhir narmadājalasaṃsthitam
vareṇa chandayāmāsa tatastuṣṭo maheśvaraḥ
varaṃ dāsyāmi deveśa varaṃ vṛṇu yathepsitam
indra uvāca
yadi tuṣṭo 'si deveśa yadi deyo varo mama
atra saṃsthāpayiṣyāmi sadā saṃnihito bhava
evamastviti coktvā taṃ brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ
jagmurākāśamāviśya stūyamānā maharṣibhiḥ
gateṣu devadeveṣu devarājaḥ śatakratuḥ
sthāpayitvā mahādevaṃ jagāma tridaśālayam
indratīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā tarpayet pitṛdevatāḥ
mahāpātakayukto 'pi mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ
indratīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayet parameśvaram
so 'śvamedhasya yajñasya puṣkalaṃ phalam aśnute
etatte kathitaṃ sarvaṃ tīrthamāhātmyamuttamam
śrutamātreṇa yenaiva mucyante pātakair narāḥ
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe indratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭādaśottaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchettu rājendra kahloḍītīrtham uttamam
revāyāścottare kūle sarvapāpavināśanam
hitārthaṃ sarvabhūtānām ṛṣibhiḥ sthāpitaṃ purā
tapasā tu samuddhṛtya narmadāyāṃ mahāmbhasi
snātvā tu kapilātīrthe kapilāṃ yaḥ prayacchati
śrutvā cākhyānakaṃ divyaṃ brāhmaṇāñchṛṇu yatphalam
sarveṣāmeva dānānāṃ kapilādānamuttamam
brāhmaṇānveṣitaṃ pūrvamṛṣidevasamāgame
sadyaḥ prasūtāṃ kapilāṃ śobhanāṃ yaḥ prayacchati
sopavāso jitakrodhastasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
sasamudraguhā tena saśailavanakānanā
dattā caiva mahābāho pṛthivī nātra saṃśayaḥ
vācikaṃ mānasaṃ pāpaṃ karmaṇā yatpurā kṛtam
naśyate kapilāṃ dattvā saptajanmārjitaṃ nṛpa
bhūmidānaṃ dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ hastyaśvakanakādikam
kapilādānasyaikasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm
tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā kapilāṃ yaḥ prayacchati
mṛto viṣṇupuraṃ yāti gīyamāno 'psarogaṇaiḥ
yāvanti tasyā romāṇi savatsāyāstu bhārata
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi sa svarge krīḍate ciram
tato 'vakīrṇakālena tviha mānuṣyatāṃ gataḥ
dhanadhānyasamopeto jāyate vipule kule
vedavidyā vratasnātaḥ sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ
vyādhiśokavinirmukto jīvecca śaradāṃ śatam
etatte sarvamākhyātaṃ kalhoḍītīrtham uttamam
yatkṛtvā sarvapāpebhyo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe kahloḍītīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikonaviṃśatyuttaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi kambukeśvaramuttamam
hiraṇyakaśipurdaityo dānavo baladarpitaḥ
avadhyaḥ sarvalokānāṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ
tasya putro mahātejāḥ prahlādo nāma nāmataḥ
viṣṇuprasādādbhaktyā ca tasya rājye pratiṣṭhitaḥ
virocanastasya sutas tasyāpi balireva ca
baliputro 'bhavad bāṇastasmādapi ca śambaraḥ
śambarasyānvaye jātaḥ kamburnāma mahāsuraḥ
jñātvā viṣṇumayaṃ ghoraṃ mahadbhayamupasthitam
dānavānāṃ vināśāya nānyo hetuḥ kadācana
sa tyaktvā putradārāṃśca suhṛdbandhuparigrahān
cacāra maunamāsthāya tapaḥ kamburmahāmatiḥ
akṣasūtrakaro bhūtvā daṇḍī muṇḍī ca mekhalī
śākayāvakabhakṣaśca valkalājinasaṃvṛtaḥ
snātvā nityaṃ dhṛtiparo narmadājalamāśritaḥ
pūjayaṃstu mahādevamarbudaṃ varṣasaṃkhyayā
tatastutoṣa bhagavāndevadevo maheśvaraḥ
uvāca dānavaṃ kāle meghagambhīrayā girā
bhobhoḥ kambo mahābhāga tuṣṭo 'haṃ tava suvrata
iṣṭaṃ vratānāṃ paramaṃ maunaṃ sarvārthasādhanam
caritaṃ ca tvayā loke devadānavaduścaram
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te yatte manasi rocate
kamburuvāca
yadi prasanno deveśa yadi deyo varo mama
akṣayyaścāvyayaścaiva svecchayā vicarāmyaham
daityadānavasaṅghānāṃ saṃyugeṣvapalāyitā
bhayaṃ cānyanna vidyeta muktvā devaṃ gadādharam
tasyāhaṃ saṃyuge sādhyo yenopāyena śaṅkara
bhavāmi na sadā kālaṃ taṃ vadasva varaṃ mama
īśvara uvāca
mama saṃnihito yatra tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi dānava
tatra viṣṇubhayaṃ nāsti vasātra vigatajvaraḥ
tasya devādhidevasya vedagarbhasya saṃyuge
śaṅkhacakradharasyeśā nāhaṃ sarve surāsurāḥ
kiṃ punaryo dviṣatyenaṃ lokālokaprabhuṃ harim
sa sukhī vartate kālaṃ na nimeṣaṃ mataṃ mama
tasmāt tvaṃ parayā bhaktyā sarvabhūtahite rataḥ
vasiṣyasi ciraṃ kālam ityuktvādarśanaṃ gataḥ
gate cādarśanaṃ deve tatra tīrthe mahāmatiḥ
sthāpayāmāsa deveśaṃ śivaṃ śāntamanāmayam
tasmiṃstīrthe mahādevaṃ sthāpayitvā divaṃ gataḥ
tadāprabhṛti tatpārtha kambutīrthamiti śrutam
vikhyātaṃ sarvalokeṣu mahāpātakanāśanam
kambutīrthe naraḥ snātvā vidhinābhyarcya bhāskaram
ṛgyajuḥsāmamantraiśca stūyamāno nṛpottama
tasya puṇyaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇairvedapāragaiḥ
tatsarvaṃ tu śṛṇuṣvādya mamaiva gadato nṛpa
ṛgyajuḥsāmagīteṣu sāṅgopāṅgeṣu yatphalam
tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti gāyatrīmātramantravit
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā tarpayet pitṛdevatāḥ
pūjayed devamīśānaṃ so 'gniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet
akāmo vā sakāmo vā tatra tīrthe kalevaram
yastyajennātra sandeho rudralokaṃ sa gacchati
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe kambukeśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma viṃśatyuttaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahīpāla candrahāsamataḥ param
yatra siddhiṃ parāṃ prāptaḥ somarājaḥ surottamaḥ
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kathaṃ siddhiṃ parāṃ prāptaḥ somanātho jagatpatiḥ
tatsarvaṃ śrotumicchāmi kathayasva mamānagha
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
purā śapto munīndreṇa dakṣeṇa kila bhārata
asevanāddhi dārāṇāṃ kṣayarogī bhaviṣyasi
udvāhitānāṃ patnīnāṃ ye na kurvanti sevanam
yā niṣṭhā jāyate nṛṇāṃ tāṃ śṛṇuṣva narādhipa
ṛtāvṛtau hi nārīṇāṃ sevanājjāyate sutaḥ
sutātsvargaśca mokṣaśca ityevaṃ śrutibhāṣitam
tatkālocitadharmeṇa veṣṭito raurave patet
tasyāstadrudhiraṃ pāpaḥ pibate kālamīpsitam
tato 'vatīrṇaḥ kālena yāṃ yāṃ yoniṃ prayāsyati
tasyāṃ tasyāṃ sa duṣṭātmā durbhago jāyate sadā
nārīṇāṃ tu sadā kāmo 'bhyadhikāḥ parivartate
viśeṣeṇa ṛtau kāle pīḍyate kāmasāyakaiḥ
paribhūtā hitā bhartrā dhyāyante 'nyaṃ patiṃ striyaḥ
tataḥ putraḥ samutpanno hyaṭate kulamuttamam
svargasthāstena pitaraḥ pūrvajāste pitāmahāḥ
patanti jātamātreṇa kulaṭastena cocyate
tena karmavipākena kṣayarogyabhavacchaśī
tyaktvā lokaṃ surendrāṇāṃ martyalokamupāgataḥ
tatastīrthānyanekāni puṇyānyāyatanāni ca
bhramanvai narmadāṃ prāptaḥ sarvapāpapraṇāśanīm
upavāsaṃ ca dānāni vratāni niyamāṃs tathā
cacāra dvādaśābdāni tato muktaḥ sa kilbiṣaiḥ
snāpayitvā mahādevaṃ sarvapātakanāśanam
jagāma prabhayā pūrṇaḥ sa ca lokamanuttamam
yenaiva sthāpito devaḥ pūjyate varṣasaṃkhyayā
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi rudraloke sa pūjyate
tena devānvidhānoktānsthāpayanti narā bhuvi
akṣayaṃ cāvyayaṃ yasmātkālaṃ bhuñjanti mānavāḥ
somatīrthe naraḥ snātvā pūjayeddevamīśvaram
sa bhrājate naro loke somavat priyadarśanaḥ
candrahāse tu yo gatvā grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ
snānaṃ samācared bhaktyā mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ
tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca candrahāse śubhāśubham
kṛtaṃ nṛpavaraśreṣṭha sarvaṃ bhavati cākṣayam
te dhanyāste mahātmānas teṣāṃ janma sujīvitam
candrahāse tu ye snātvā paśyanti grahaṇaṃ narāḥ
vācikaṃ mānasaṃ pāpaṃ karmajaṃ yatpurākṛtam
snānamātreṇa rājendra tatra tīrthe praṇaśyati
bahavastaṃ na jānanti mahāmohasamanvitāḥ
dehasthamiva sarveṣāṃ paramānandarūpiṇam
paścime sāgare gatvā somatīrthe tu yatphalam
tatsamagram avāpnoti candrahāse na saṃśayaḥ
saṃkrāntau ca vyatīpāte ayane viṣuve tathā
candrahāse naraḥ snātvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
te mūḍhāste durācārāsteṣāṃ janma nirarthakam
candrahāsaṃ na jānanti ye revāyāṃ vyavasthitam
candrahāse tu yaḥ kaścitsaṃnyāsaṃ kurute dvijaḥ
anivartikā gatistasya somalokānna saṃśayaḥ
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe somatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikaviṃśatyuttaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahīpāla kohanasveti viśrutam
sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ tīrthaṃ mṛtyuvināśanam
purā tatra dvijaḥ kaścidvedavedāṅgapāragaḥ
patnīputrasuhṛdvargaiḥ svakarmanirato 'vasat
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
brāhmaṇasya tu yatkarma utpattiḥ kṣatriyasya tu
vaiśyasyāpi ca śūdrasya tatsarvaṃ kathayasva me
dharmasyārhasya kāmasya mokṣasya ca paraṃ vidhim
nikhilaṃ jñātum icchāmi nānyo vettā matirmama
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
utpattikāraṇaṃ brahmā devadevaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
prathamaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ carācarajagadguruḥ
dvijātayo mukhājjātāḥ kṣatriyā bāhuyantrataḥ
ūrupradeśād vaiśyāstu śūdrāḥ pādeṣvathābhavan
tatastvanye pṛthagvarṇāḥ pṛthagdharmān samācaran
paryāyeṇa samutpannā hyanulomavilomataḥ
teṣāṃ dharmaṃ pravakṣyāmi śrutismṛtyarthacoditam
yena samyakkṛtenaiva sarve yānti parāṃ gatim
gatirdhyānaṃ vinā bhaktair brāhmaṇaiḥ prāpyate nṛpa
adhyāpayanyato vedānvedaṃ vāpi yathāvidhi
kulajāṃ rūpasampannāṃ sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitām
udvāhayettataḥ patnīṃ guruṇānumate tadā
tataḥ smārtaṃ vivāhāgniṃ śrautaṃ vā pūjayet kramāt
pratigrahadhano bhūtvā dambhalobhavivarjitaḥ
pañcayajñavidhānāni kārayedvai yathāvidhi
vanaṃ gacchet tataḥ paścāddvitīyāśramasevanāt
putreṣu bhāryāṃ nikṣipya sarvasaṅgavivarjitaḥ
iṣṭāṃllokānavāpnoti na ceha jāyate punaḥ
kṣatriyastu sthito rājye pālayitvā vasuṃdharām
śaśvaddharmamanāścaiva prāpnoti paramāṃ gatim
vaiśyadharmo na sandehaḥ kṛṣigorakṣaṇe rataḥ
satyaśaucasamopeto gacchate svargamuttamam
na śūdrasya pṛthagdharmo vihitaḥ parameṣṭhinā
na mantro na ca saṃskāro na vidyāparisevanam
na śabdavidyāsamayo devatābhyarcanāni ca
yathā jātena satataṃ vartitavyamaharniśam
sa dharmaḥ sarvavarṇānāṃ purā sṛṣṭaḥ svayambhuvā
mantrasaṃskārasampannāstrayo varṇā dvijātayaḥ
teṣāṃ matam anādṛtya yadi varteta kāmataḥ
sa mṛto jāyate śvā vai gatirūrdhvā na vidyate
na teṣāṃ preṣaṇaṃ nityaṃ teṣāṃ matamanusmaran
yaśobhāgī svadharmasthaḥ svargabhāgī sa jāyate
evaṃ guṇagaṇākīrṇo 'vasadvipraḥ sa bhārata
hanasveti hanasveti śṛṇoti vākyamīdṛśam
tato nirīkṣate cordhvam adhaścaiva diśo daśa
vepamānaḥ sa bhītaśca praskhalaṃśca pade pade
śṛṅkhalāyudhahastaiśca pāśaiścaiva sudāruṇaiḥ
veṣṭitaṃ mahiṣārūḍhaṃ naraṃ paśyati manmukham
kṛṣṇāṃjanacayaprakhyaṃ kṛṣṇāmbaravibhūṣitam
raktākṣamāyatabhujaṃ sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitam
dṛṣṭvā taṃ tu samāyāntaṃ nirīkṣyātmānamātmanā
japañjāpyaṃ ca paramaṃ śatarudrīyasaṃstavam
tataḥ provāca bhagavānyamaḥ saṃyamano mahān
śṛṇu vākyamato brahmanyamo 'haṃ sarvajantuṣu
saṃharasva mahābhāga rudrajāpyaṃ sudurbhidam
yenāhaṃ kālapāśaistvāṃ saṃyamāmi gatavyathaḥ
tacchrutvā niṣṭhuraṃ vākyaṃ yamasya mukhanirgatam
mahābhayasamopeto brāhmaṇaḥ prapalāyitaḥ
tasya mārge gatāḥ sarve yamena saha kiṃkarāḥ
tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti taṃ vipramūcuste so 'pyadhāvata
tvaramāṇaḥ pariśrānto hā hato 'haṃ durātmabhiḥ
rakṣa rakṣa mahādeva śaraṇāgatavatsala
evamuktvāpatadbhūmau liṅgamāliṅgya bhārata
gatasattvaḥ sa viprendraḥ samāśritya sureśvaram
taṃ dṛṣṭvā patitaṃ bhūmau devadevo maheśvaraḥ
ko haniṣyati mābhaistvaṃ huṅkāramakarottadā
tena te kiṃkarāḥ sarve yamena saha bhārata
huṅkāreṇa gatāḥ sarve meghā vātahatā yathā
tadāprabhṛti tattīrthaṃ kohanasveti viśrutam
sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvatīrtheṣvanuttamam
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayet parameśvaram
agniṣṭomasya yajñasya phalamāpnotyanuttamam
tatra tīrthe tu rājendra prāṇatyāgaṃ karoti yaḥ
na paśyati yamaṃ devamityevaṃ śaṅkaro 'bravīt
agnipraveśaṃ yaḥ kuryājjale vā nṛpasattama
agniloke vaset tāvad yāvat kalpaśatatrayam
evaṃ varuṇaloke 'pi vasitvā kālamīpsitam
iha lokamanuprāpto mahādhanapatirbhavet
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe kohanatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma dvāviṃśatyuttaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchettu rājendra karmadītīrtham uttamam
yatra tiṣṭhati vighneśo gaṇanātho mahābalaḥ
tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā caturthyāṃ vā hyupoṣitaḥ
vighnaṃ na vidyate tasya saptajanmani bhārata
tatra tīrthe hi yatkiṃcid dīyate nṛpasattama
tadakṣayaphalaṃ sarvaṃ jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe karmadeśvaratīrthamāhatmyavarṇanaṃ nāma trayoviṃśatyuttaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahīpāla narmadeśvaramuttamam
tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ
agnipraveśaśca jale 'thavā mṛtyuranāśake
anivartikā gatistasya yathā me śaṅkaro 'bravīt
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe narmadeśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma caturviṃśatyuttaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahīpāla ravitīrthamanuttamam
yatra devaḥ sahasrāṃśustapastaptvā divaṃ gataḥ
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kathaṃ devo jagaddhātā sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ
tapastapati deveśastāpaso bhāskaro raviḥ
ārādhyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sarvadevaiśca pūjitaḥ
pratyakṣo dṛśyate loke sṛṣṭisaṃhārakārakaḥ
ādityatvaṃ kathaṃ prāptaḥ kathaṃ bhāskara ucyate
sarvametatsamāsena kathayasva mamānagha
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
mahāpraśno mahārāja yastvayā paripṛcchitaḥ
tatsarvaṃ sampravakṣyāmi namaskṛtya svayambhuvam
āsīdidaṃ tamobhūtamaprajñātamalakṣaṇam
apratarkyam avijñeyaṃ prasuptam iva sarvataḥ
tatas tejaśca divyaṃ ca taptapiṇḍamanuttamam
ākāśāttu yathaivolkā sṛṣṭihetor adhomukhī
tattejaso 'ntaḥ puruṣaḥ saṃjātaḥ sarvabhūṣitaḥ
sa śivo 'pāṇipādaśca yena sarvamidaṃ tatam
tasyotpannasya bhūtasya tejo rūpasya bhārata
paścātprajāpatirbhūyaḥ kālaḥ kālāntareṇa vai
agnirjātaḥ sa bhūtānāṃ manuṣyāsurarakṣasām
sarvadevādhidevaśca ādityastena cocyate
ādau tasya namaskāro 'nyeṣāṃ ca tadanantaram
kriyate daivataiḥ sarvaistena sarvairmaharṣibhiḥ
tisraḥ sandhyāstrayo devāḥ sāṃnidhyāḥ sūryamaṇḍale
namaskṛtena sūryeṇa sarve devā namaskṛtāḥ
na divā na bhaved rātriḥ ṣaṇmāsā dakṣiṇāyanam
ayanaṃ cottaraṃ cāpi bhāskareṇa vinā nṛpa
snānaṃ dānaṃ japo homaḥ svādhyāyo devatārcanam
na vartate vinā sūryaṃ tena pūjyatamo raviḥ
śabdagāḥ śrutimukhyāśca brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ
pratyakṣo bhagavāndevo dṛśyate lokapāvanaḥ
utpattiḥ pralayasthānaṃ nidhānaṃ bījamavyayam
hetureko jagannātho nānyo vidyeta bhāskarāt
evamātmabhavaṃ kṛtvā jagatsthāvarajaṅgamam
lokānāṃ tu hitārthāya sthāpayed dharmapaddhatim
narmadātaṭamāśritya sthāpayitvātmanas tanum
sahasrāṃśuṃ nidhiṃ dhāmnāṃ jagāmākāśamavyayam
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayet parameśvaram
sahasrakiraṇaṃ devaṃ nāmamantravidhānataḥ
tena taptaṃ hutaṃ tena tena sarvamanuṣṭhitam
tena samyagvidhānena samprāptaṃ paramaṃ padam
te dhanyāste mahātmānasteṣāṃ janma sujīvitam
snātvā ye narmadātoye devaṃ paśyanti bhāskaram
tathā devasya rājendra ye kurvanti pradakṣiṇam
ananyabhaktyā satataṃ trirakṣarasamanvitāḥ
tena pūtaśarīrāste mantreṇa gatapātakāḥ
yatpuṇyaṃ ca bhavet teṣāṃ tadihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu
sasamudraguhā tena saśailavanakānanā
pradakṣiṇīkṛtā sarvā pṛthivī nātra saṃśayaḥ
mantramūlam idaṃ sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram
tena mantravihīnaṃ tu kāryaṃ loke na sidhyati
yathā kāṣṭhamayo hastī yathā carmamayo mṛgaḥ
kāryārthaṃ naiva sidhyeta tathā karma hyamantrakam
bhasmahutaṃ pārtha yathā toyavivarjitam
niṣphalaṃ jāyate dānaṃ tathā mantravivarjitam
kāṣṭhapāṣāṇaloṣṭeṣu mṛnmayeṣu viśeṣataḥ
mantreṇa loke pūjāṃ tu kurvanti na hyamantrataḥ
dvādaśābdānnamaskārādbhaktyā yallabhate phalam
mantrayuktanamaskārātsakṛttallabhate phalam
saṃkrāntau ca vyatīpāte ayane viṣuve tathā
narmadāyā jale snātvā yastu pūjayate ravim
dvādaśābdena yat pāpam ajñānajñānasaṃcitam
tatkṣaṇānnaśyate sarvaṃ vahninā tu tuṣaṃ yathā
candrasūryagrahe snātvā sopavāso jitendriyaḥ
tatrādityamukhaṃ dṛṣṭvā mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ
māghamāse tu samprāpte saptamyāṃ nṛpasattama
sopavāso jitakrodha uṣitvā sūryamandire
prātaḥ snātvā vidhānena dadātyarghaṃ divākare
vidhinā mantrayuktena sa labhet puṇyamuttamam
pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇāṃ kṛtvā hyudakatarpaṇam
mandire devadevasya tataḥ pūjāṃ samācaret
gandhaiḥ puṣpaistathā dhūpairdīpanaivedyaśobhanaiḥ
pūjayitvā jagannāthaṃ tato mantramudīrayet
viṣṇuḥ śakro yamo dhātā mitro 'tha varuṇastathā
vivasvānsavitā pūṣā caṇḍāṃśurbharga eva ca
iti dvādaśanāmāni japankṛtvā pradakṣiṇām
yatphalaṃ labhate pārtha tadihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu
daridro vyādhito mūko badhiro jaḍa eva ca
na bhavetsapta janmāni ityevaṃ śaṅkaro 'bravīt
evaṃ jñātvā vidhānena japanmantraṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ
ārādhayed raviṃ bhaktyā ya icchetpuṇyamuttamam
mantrahīnāṃ tu yaḥ kuryād bhaktiṃ devasya bhārata
sa viḍambati cātmānaṃ paśukīṭapataṅgavat
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ kaścit tyajate dehamuttamam
sa gatastatra devaistu pūjyamāno maharṣibhiḥ
svecchayā suciraṃ kālamiha loke nṛpo bhavet
putrapautrasamāyukto hastyaśvarathasaṅkulaḥ
dāsīdāsaśatopeto jāyate vipule kule
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe ravitīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma pañcaviṃśatyuttaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchettu rājendra paraṃ tīrthamayonijam
snātamātro narastatra na paśyed yonisaṅkaṭam
tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā pūjayed devamīśvaram
ayonijo mahādeva yathā tvaṃ parameśvara
tathā mocaya māṃ deva sambhavād yonisaṅkaṭāt
gandhapuṣpādidhūpaiśca sa mucyet sarvapātakaiḥ
tasya devasya yo bhaktyā kurute liṅgapūraṇam
sa vaseddevadevasya yāvatsikthasya saṃkhyayā
ayonije mahādevaṃ snāpayed gandhavāriṇā
madhukṣīreṇa dadhnā vā sa labhed vipulāṃ śriyam
aṣṭabhyāṃ ca site pakṣe asitāṃ vā caturdaśīm
pūjayitvā mahādevaṃ prīṇayed gītavādyakaiḥ
vasetsa ca śive loke ye kurvanti manoharam
te vasanti śive loke yāvad ābhūtasamplavam
tasya devasya bhaktyā tu yaḥ karoti pradakṣiṇām
vijñāpayaṃśca satataṃ mantreṇānena bhārata
tasya yatphalamuddiṣṭaṃ pāramparyeṇa mānavaiḥ
sakāśāddevadevasya tacchṛṇuṣva samādhinā
ayonijo mahādeva yathā tvaṃ parameśvara
tathā mocaya māṃ śarva sambhavādyonisaṅkaṭāt
kiṃ tasya bahubhirmantraiḥ kaṃṭhaśoṣaṇatatparaiḥ
yenauṃnamaḥ śivāyeti proktaṃ devasya saṃnidhau
tenādhītaṃ śrutaṃ tena tena sarvamanuṣṭhitam
yenauṃnamaḥ śivāyeti mantrābhyāsaḥ sthirīkṛtaḥ
na tatphalamavāpnoti sarvadeveṣu vai dvijaḥ
yatphalaṃ samavāpnoti ṣaḍakṣara udīraṇāt
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayecchivayoginam
dvijānāmayutaṃ sāgraṃ sa labhet phalamuttamam
athavā bhaktiyuktastu teṣāṃ dānte jitendriye
saṃskṛtya dadate bhikṣāṃ phalaṃ tasya tato 'dhikam
yatihaste jalaṃ dadyād bhikṣāṃ dattvā punarjalam
sā bhikṣā meruṇā tulyā tajjalaṃ sāgaropamam
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe ayoniprabhavatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaḍviṃśatyuttaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra agnitīrthamanuttamam
tatra snātvā tu pakṣādau mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ kanyāṃ dadyāt svayamalaṃkṛtām
tasya yatphalamuddiṣṭaṃ tacchṛṇuṣva narottama
agniṣṭomātirātrābhyāṃ śataṃ śataguṇīkṛtam
prāpnoti puruṣo dattvā yathāśaktyā hyalaṃkṛtām
tasyāḥ putraprapautrāṇāṃ yā bhaved romasaṃgatiḥ
sa yāti tena mānena śivaloke parāṃ gatim
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe agnitīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma saptaviṃśatyuttaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchettu rājendra bhṛkuṭeśvaram uttamam
yatra siddho mahābhāgo bhṛguḥ paramakopanaḥ
tena varṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ tapaścīrṇaṃ purānagha
putrārthaṃ varayāmāsa putraṃ putravatāṃ varaḥ
varo datto mahābhāga devenāndhakaghātinā
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayet parameśvaram
agniṣṭomasya yajñasya phalamaṣṭaguṇaṃ labhet
bhṛkuṭeśaṃ tu yaḥ kaścid ghṛtena madhunā saha
putrārthī snāpayed bhaktyā sa labhet putramīpsitam
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā dadyād viprāya kāñcanam
godānaṃ vā mahīṃ vāpi tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
sasamudraguhā tena saśailavanakānanā
dattā pṛthvī na sandehas tena sarvā nṛpottama
tena dānena sa svarge krīḍayitvā yathāsukham
martye bhavati rājendro brāhmaṇo vā supūjitaḥ
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe bhṛkuṭeśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭāviṃśatyuttaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchen mahīpāla brahmatīrthamanuttamam
anyeṣāṃ caiva tīrthānāṃ parātparataraṃ mahat
tatra tīrthe suraśreṣṭho brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
caturṇāmapi varṇānāṃ narmadātaṭamāśritaḥ
vācikaṃ mānasaṃ pāpaṃ karmajaṃ yatpurākṛtam
tatkṣālayati deveśo darśanād eva pātakam
śrutismṛtyuditānyeva tatra snātvā dvijarṣabhāḥ
prāyaścittāni kurvanti teṣāṃ vāsastriviṣṭape
ye punaḥ śāstramutsṛjya kāmalobhaprapīḍitāḥ
prāyaścittaṃ vadiṣyanti te vai nirayagāminaḥ
snātvādau pātakī brahmannatvā tu kīrtayed agham
tasya tannaśyate kṣipraṃ tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayet pitṛdevatāḥ
agniṣṭomasya yajñasya sa labhet phalamuttamam
tatra tīrthe tu yad dānaṃ brahmoddiśya prayacchati
tadakṣayaphalaṃ sarvamityevaṃ śaṅkaro 'bravīt
gāyatrīsāramātro 'pi tatra yaḥ kriyate japaḥ
ṛgyajuḥsāmasahitaḥ sa bhavennātra saṃśayaḥ
tatra tīrthe tu yo bhaktyā tyajeddehaṃ sudustyajam
anivartikā gatistasya brahmalokān na saṃśayaḥ
yāvadasthīni tiṣṭhanti brahmatīrthe ca dehinām
tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi devaloke mahīyate
avatīrṇastato loke brahmajño jāyate kule
uttamaḥ sarvavarṇānāṃ devānāmiva devatā
vidyāsthānāni sarvāṇi vetti vedāṅgapāragaḥ
jāyate pūjito loke rājabhiḥ sa na saṃśayaḥ
putrapautrasamopetaḥ sarvavyādhivivarjitaḥ
jīvedvarṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ brahmatīrthaprabhāvataḥ
etatpuṇyaṃ pāpaharaṃ tīrthaṃ jñānavatāṃ varam
ye paśyanti mahātmāno hyamṛtatvaṃ prayānti te
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe brahmatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikonatriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
narmadādakṣiṇe kūle devatīrthamanuttamam
tatra devaiḥ samāgatya toṣitaḥ parameśvaraḥ
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā kāmakrodhavivarjitaḥ
sa labhennātra sandeho gosahasraphalaṃ dhruvam
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe devatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma triṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
narmadādakṣiṇe kūle nāgatīrthamanuttamam
yatra siddhā mahānāgā bhaye jāte tato nṛpa
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
mahābhayānāṃ lokasya nāgānāṃ dvijasattama
kathaṃ jātaṃ bhayaṃ tīvraṃ yena te tapasi sthitāḥ
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyacca yatsurāsuramānave
tāta te viditaṃ sarvaṃ tena me kautukaṃ mahat
mama saṃtāpajaṃ duḥkhaṃ duryodhanasamudbhavam
tava vaktrāmbujaughena plāvitaṃ nirvṛtiṃ gatam
śrutvā tava mukhodgītāṃ kathāṃ pāpapraṇāśanīm
bhūyo bhūyaḥ smṛtirjātā śravaṇe mama suvrata
na kleśatvaṃ dvije yuktaṃ na cānyo jānate phalam
vidyādānasya mahataḥ śrāvitasya sutasya ca
evaṃ jñātvā yathānyāyaṃ yaḥ praśnaḥ pṛcchito mayā
kathā tu kathyatāṃ vipra dayāṃ kṛtvā mamopari
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
yathā yathā tvaṃ nṛpa bhāṣase ca tathā tathā me sukhameti bhāratī
śaithilyabhāvājjarayānvitasya tvatsauhṛdaṃ naśyati naiva tāta
kathayāmi yathāvṛttam itihāsaṃ purātanam
kathitaṃ pūrvato vṛddhaiḥ pāramparyeṇa bhārata
dve bhārye kaśyapasyāstāṃ sarvalokeṣvanuttame
garutmato vai vinatā sarpāṇāṃ kadrureva ca
aśvasaṃdarśanāt tābhyāṃ kalirūpaṃ vyavasthitam
prabhātakāle rājendra bhāskarākāravarcasam
taṃ dṛṣṭvā vinatā rūpam aśvaṃ sarvatra pāṇḍuram
atha tāṃ kadrūmavocatsā paśya paśya varānane
uccaiḥśravasaḥ sādṛśyaṃ paśya sarvatra pāṇḍuram
dhāvamānam aviśrāntaṃ javena pavanopamam
taṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasā yāntam īrṣyābhāvena mohitā
kṛṣṇaṃ matvā tathājalpattayā saha nṛpottama
vinate tvaṃ mṛṣā loke nṛśaṃse kulapāṃsani
kṛṣṇaṃ cainaṃ vada śvetaṃ narakaṃ yāsyase param
vinatovāca
satyānṛte tu vacane paṇo 'yaṃ te mamaiva tu
sahasraṃ vatsarāndāsī bhaveyaṃ tava veśmani
tatheti te pratijñāya rātrau gatvā svakaṃ gṛham
parityajya ubhe te tu krodhamūrchitamūrchite
bandhugarvasya gatvā tu kathayāmāsa taṃ paṇam
kadrūrvinatayā sārddhaṃ yadvṛttaṃ pramadālaye
tacchrutvā bāndhavāḥ sarve kadrūputrāstathaiva ca
na manyante hitaṃ kāryaṃ kṛtaṃ mātrā vigarhitam
akṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇatām amba kathaṃ gaccheddhayottamaḥ
dāsatvaṃ prāpsyase tvaṃ hi paṇenānena suvrate
kadrūruvāca
bhaveyaṃ na yathādāsī tatkurudhvaṃ hi satvaram
viśadhvaṃ romakūpeṣu tasyāśvasya matirmama
kṣaṇamātraṃ kṛte kārye sā dāsī ca bhavenmama
tataḥ svasthoragāḥ sarve bhaviṣyatha yathāsukham
sarpā ūcuḥ
yathā tvaṃ jananī devi pannagānāṃ matā bhuvi
tathāpi sā viśeṣeṇa vañcitavyā na karhicit
kadrūruvāca
mama vākyamakurvāṇā ye kecidbhuvi pannagāḥ
havyavāhamukhaṃ sarve te yāsyantyavicāritāḥ
etacchrutvā tu vacanaṃ ghoraṃ mātṛmukhodbhavam
kecitpraviṣṭā romāṇi tathānye girisaṃsthitāḥ
kecitpraviṣṭā jāhnavyāmanye ca tapasi sthitāḥ
tato varṣasahasrānte tutoṣa parameśvaraḥ
mahādevo jagaddhātā hyuvāca parayā girā
bho bhoḥ sarpā nivartadhvaṃ tapaso 'sya mahatphalam
yamicchatha dadāmyadya nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
sarpā ūcuḥ
kadrūśāpabhayādbhītā devadeva maheśvara
tava pārśve vasiṣyāmo yāvadābhūtasamplavam
devadeva uvāca
ekaścāyaṃ mahābāhurvāsukirbhujagottamaḥ
mama pārśve vasennityaṃ sarveṣāṃ bhayarakṣakaḥ
anyeṣāṃ caiva sarpāṇāṃ bhayaṃ nāsti mamājñayā
āplutya narmadātoye bhujagāste ca rakṣitāḥ
nāsti mṛtyubhayaṃ teṣāṃ vasadhvaṃ yatra cepsitam
kadrūśāpabhayaṃ nāsti hyeṣa me vistaraḥ paraḥ
evaṃ dattvā varaṃ teṣāṃ devadevo maheśvaraḥ
jagāmākāśamāviśya kailāsaṃ dharaṇīdharam
gate cādarśanaṃ deve vāsukipramukhā nṛpa
sthāpayitvā tathā jagmurdevadevaṃ maheśvaram
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ kaścit pañcamyāmarcayecchivam
tasya nāgakulānyaṣṭau na hiṃsanti kadācana
mṛtaḥ kālena mahatā tatra tīrthe nareśvara
śivasyānucaro bhūtvā vasate kālamīpsitam
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe nāgeśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikatriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchettu rājendra uttare narmadātaṭe
sarvapāpaharaṃ tīrthaṃ vārāhaṃ nāma nāmataḥ
tatra devo jagaddhātā vārāhaṃ rūpam āsthitaḥ
sthito lokahitārthāya saṃsārārṇavatārakaḥ
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayed dharaṇīdharam
gandhamālyaviśeṣaiśca jayaśabdādimaṅgalaiḥ
upavāsaparo bhūtvā dvādaśyāṃ nṛpasattama
vṛṣalāḥ pāpakarmāṇas tathaivāndhapiśācinaḥ
ālāpād gātrasaṃparkān niḥśvāsāt sahabhojanāt
pāpaṃ saṃkramate yasmāt tasmāt tān parivarjayet
brāhmaṇān pūjayed bhaktyā yathāśaktyā yathāvidhi
rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ kāryaṃ kathāyāṃ tatra bhārata
prabhāte vimale snātvā tatra tīrthe jagadgurum
ye paśyanti jitakrodhāste muktāḥ sarvapātakaiḥ
yathā tu dṛṣṭvā bhujagāḥ suparṇaṃ naśyanti muktvā viṣamugratejaḥ
naśyanti pāpāni tathaiva śīghraṃ dṛṣṭvā mukhaṃ śūkararūpiṇastu
nabhogataṃ naśyati cāndhakāraṃ dṛṣṭvā raviṃ devavaraṃ tathaiva
naśyanti pāpāni sudustarāṇi dṛṣṭvā mukhaṃ pārtha dharādharasya
kiṃ tasya bahubhir mantrair bhaktir yasya janārdane
namo nārāyaṇāyeti mantraḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ
eko 'pi kṛṣṇasya kṛtaḥ praṇāmo daśāśvamedhāvabhṛthena tulyaḥ
daśāśvamedhī punareti janma kṛṣṇapraṇāmī na punarbhavāya
dhyāyamānā mahātmāno rūpaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ hareḥ
ye tyajanti svakaṃ dehaṃ tatra tīrthe jitendriyāḥ
te gacchantyamalaṃ sthānaṃ yatsurair api durlabham
kṣarākṣaravinirmuktaṃ tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe ādivārāhatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma dvātriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahīpāla paraṃ tīrthacatuṣṭayam
yeṣāṃ darśanamātreṇa sarvapāpakṣayo bhavet
kauberaṃ vāruṇaṃ yāmyaṃ vāyavyaṃ tu tataḥ param
yatra siddhā mahāprājñā lokapālā mahābalāḥ
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kimarthaṃ lokapālaiśca tapaścīrṇaṃ purānagha
narmadātaṭamāśritya hyetanme vaktumarhasi
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
adhiṣṭhānaṃ samicchanti hyacalaṃ nirbale sati
saṃsāre sarvabhūtānāṃ tṛṇabinduvadasthire
kadalīsāraniḥsāre mṛgatṛṣṇeva cañcale
sthāvare jaṅgame sarve bhūtagrāme caturvidhe
dharmo mātā pitā dharmo dharmo bandhuḥ suhṛt tathā
ādhāraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ trailokye sacarācare
evaṃ jñātvā tu te sarve lokapālāḥ kṛtakṣaṇāḥ
tapaste cakruratulaṃ mārutāhāratatparāḥ
tatastuṣṭo mahādevaḥ kṛtasyārddhe gate tadā
anurūpeṇa rājendra yugasya parameśvaraḥ
vareṇa chandayāmāsa lokapālān mahābalān
yo yamicchati kāmaṃ vai taṃ taṃ tasya dadāmyaham
etacchrutvā vacastasya lokapālā jagaddhitāḥ
varadaṃ prārthayāmāsur devaṃ varam anuttamam
kubera uvāca
yadi tuṣṭo mahādeva yadi deyo varo mama
yakṣāṇām īśvaraścāhaṃ bhavāmi dhanadastviti
tataḥ provāca deveśaṃ yamaḥ saṃyamane rataḥ
tatra pradhāno bhagavān bhaveyaṃ sarvajantuṣu
varuṇo 'nantaraṃ prāha praṇamya tu maheśvaram
krīḍeyaṃ vāruṇe loke yādogaṇasamanvitaḥ
jagādāśu tato vāyuḥ praṇamya tu maheśvaram
vyāpakatvaṃ trilokeṣu prārthayāmāsa bhārata
teṣāṃ yadīpsitaṃ kāmamumayā saha śaṅkaraḥ
sarveṣāṃ lokapālānaḥ dattvā cādarśanaṃ gataḥ
gate maheśvare deve yathāsthānaṃ tu te sthitāḥ
sthāpanā ca kṛtā sarvaiḥ svanāmnaiva pṛthakpṛthak
kuberaśca kubereśaṃ yamaścaiva yameśvaram
varuṇo varuṇeśaṃ tu vāto vāteśvaraṃ nṛpa
tarpaṇaṃ vidadhuḥ sarve mantraiśca vividhaiḥ śubhaiḥ
sarve sarveśvaraṃ deva pūjayitvā yathāvidhi
āhvayāmāsus tān viprānsarve sarveśvarā iva
kṣāntadāntajitakrodhānsarvabhūtābhayapradān
vedavidyāvratasnātān sarvaśāstraviśāradān
ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃyuktāṃs tathātharvavibhūṣitān
cāturvidhyaṃ tu sarveṣāṃ dānaṃ dāsyāma gṛhṇata
evamuktvā tu sarveṣāṃ viprāṇāṃ dānamuttamam
tatra sthāne dadus teṣāṃ bhūmidānam anuttamam
yāvaccandraśca sūryaśca yāvat tiṣṭhati medinī
tāvaddānaṃ tu yuṣmākaṃ paripanthī na kaścana
rājā vā rājatulyo vā lokapālair anuttamam
dattaṃ lopayate mūḍhaḥ śrūyatāṃ tasya yo vidhiḥ
śoṣayeddhanado vittaṃ tasya pāpasya bhārata
śarīraṃ varuṇo devaḥ saṃtatīṃ śvasanas tathā
āyurnayati tasyāśu yamaḥ saṃyamano mahān
niḥśeṣaṃ bhasmasāt kṛtvā hutabhugyāti bhārata
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena brāhmaṇebhyo yudhiṣṭhira
bhaktiḥ kāryā nṛpaiḥ sarvair icchadbhiḥ śreya ātmanaḥ
rājā vṛkṣo brāhmaṇāstasya mūlaṃ bhṛtyāḥ parṇā mantriṇastasya śākhāḥ
tasmān mūlaṃ yatnato rakṣaṇīyaṃ mūle gupte nāsti vṛkṣasya nāśaḥ
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi svarge tiṣṭhati bhūmidaḥ
ācchettā cāvamantā ca tānyeva narake vaset
svadattā paradattā vā pālanīyā vasuṃdharā
yasya yasya yadā bhūmistasya tasya tadā phalam
devatājñāmanusmṛtya rājāno ye 'pi tāṃ nṛpa
pālayiṣyanti satataṃ teṣāṃ vāsastriviṣṭape
svadattā paradattā vā yatnādrakṣyā yudhiṣṭhira
mahī mahīkṣitā nityaṃ dānācchreyo 'nupālanam
āyuryaśo balaṃ vittaṃ saṃtatiścākṣayā nṛpa
teṣāṃ bhaviṣyate nūnaṃ ye prajāpālane ratāḥ
evamuktvā tu tān sarvāṃllokapālān dvijottamān
pūjayitvā vidhānena praṇipatya vyasarjayan
gateṣu vipramukhyeṣu snātvā hutahutāśanāḥ
lokapālāḥ kṣudhāviṣṭāḥ paryaṭanbhaikṣamātmanaḥ
asthicarmāvaśeṣāṅgāḥ kapāloddhṛtapāṇayaḥ
alabdhagrāsamarddhārdhaṃ niryayur nagarādbahiḥ
śāpaṃ dattvā tadā krodhād brāhmaṇāya yudhiṣṭhira
daridrāḥ satataṃ mūrkhā bhaveyuśca yayurgṛhān
tadāprabhṛti te sarve brāhmaṇā dhanavarjitāḥ
śāpadoṣeṇa kauberyāṃ saṃjātā duḥkhabhājanāḥ
na dhanaṃ paitṛkaṃ putrairna pitā putrapautrikam
bhuñjate sakalaṃ kālamityevaṃ śaṅkaro 'bravīt
kubereśo naraḥ snātvā yastu pūjayate śivam
gandhadhūpanamaskāraiḥ so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet
yamatīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā sampaśyati yameśvaram
sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyeta saptajanmāntarārjitaiḥ
pūrṇamāsyām amāvāsyāṃ snātvā tu pitṛtarpaṇam
yaḥ karoti tilaiḥ snānaṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
sutṛptāstena toyena pitaraśca pitāmahāḥ
svargasthā dvādaśābdāni krīḍanti prapitāmahāḥ
varuṇeśe naraḥ snātvā hyarcayitvā maheśvaram
vājapeyasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoti puṣkalam
mṛtāṃ kālena mahatā loke yatra jaleśvaraḥ
sa gacchet tatra yānena gīyamāno 'psarogaṇaiḥ
vāteśvare naraḥ snātvā sampūjya ca maheśvaram
jāyate kṛtakṛtyo 'sau lokapālānavekṣayan
kiṃ tasya bahubhiryajñairdānairvā bahudakṣiṇaiḥ
snātvā catuṣṭaye loke avāptaṃ janmanaḥ phalam
te dhanyāste mahātmānas teṣāṃ janma sujīvitam
nityaṃ vasanti kaurilyāṃ lokapālānnimantrya ye
etatpuṇyaṃ pāpaharaṃ dhanyamāyurvivardhanam
paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ caiva sarvapāpakṣayo bhavet
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe kuberāditīrthacatuṣṭayamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma trayastriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
narmadādakṣiṇe kūle rāmeśvaramanuttamam
tīrthaṃ pāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvaduḥkhaghnamuttamam
tatra tīrthe tu ye snātvā pūjayanti maheśvaram
mahādevaṃ mahātmānaṃ mucyante sarvakilbiṣaiḥ
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe rāmeśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma catustriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tasyaivānantaraṃ cānyatsiddheśvaramanuttamam
tīrthaṃ sarvaguṇopetaṃ sarvalokeṣu pūjitam
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā hyumārudraṃ prapūjayet
vājapeyasya yajñasya sa labhet phalamuttamam
tena puṇyena mahatā mṛtaḥ svargamavāpnuyāt
apsarogaṇasaṃvīto jayaśabdādimaṅgalaiḥ
sahasravatsarāṃstatra krīḍayitvā yathāsukham
dhanadhānyasamopete kule mahati jāyate
pūjyamāno naraśreṣṭha vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ
vyādhiśokavinirmukto jīvecca śaradāṃ śatam
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe siddheśvaramāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma pañcatriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahīpāla cāhalyeśvaramuttamam
yatra siddhā mahābhāgā tvahalyā tāpasī purā
gautamo brāhmaṇastvāsīt sākṣād brahmeva cāparaḥ
satyadharmasamāyukto vānaprasthāśrame rataḥ
tasya patnī mahābhāgā hyahalyā nāma viśrutā
rūpayauvanasampannā triṣu lokeṣu viśrutā
asyā apyatirūpeṇa devarājaḥ śatakratuḥ
mohito lobhayāmāsa hyahalyāṃ balasūdanaḥ
māṃ bhajasva varārohe devarājam anindite
krīḍayasva mayā sārddhaṃ triṣu lokeṣu pūjitā
kiṃ kariṣyasi vipreṇa śaucācārakṛśena tu
tapaḥsvādhyāyaśīlena kliśyantīva sulocane
evamuktā varārohā strīsvabhāvāt sucañcalā
manasādhyāya śakraṃ sā kāmena kaluṣīkṛtā
tasyā viditvā taṃ bhāvaṃ sa devaḥ pākaśāsanaḥ
gautamaṃ vañcayāmāsa duṣṭabhāvena bhāvitaḥ
viditvā cāntaraṃ tasya gṛhītvā veṣamuttamam
ahalyāṃ ramayāmāsa viśvastāṃ mandirāntike
kṣaṇamātrāntare tatra devarājasya bhārata
ājagāma muniśreṣṭho mandiraṃ tvarayānvitaḥ
āgataṃ gautamaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhītabhītaḥ puraṃdaraḥ
nirgataḥ sa tato dṛṣṭvā śakro 'yamiti cintayan
tataḥ śaśāpa devendraṃ gautamaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
ajitendriyo 'si yasmāttvaṃ tasmād bahubhago bhava
evamuktastu devendrastatkṣaṇādeva bhārata
bhagānāṃ tu sahasreṇa tatkṣaṇād eva veṣṭitaḥ
tyaktvā rājyaṃ suraiḥ sārddhaṃ gataśrīko jagāma ha
tapaścacāra vipulaṃ gautamena mahītale
ahalyāpi tataḥ śaptā yasmāt tvaṃ duṣṭacāriṇī
prekṣya māṃ ramase śakraṃ tasmād aśmamayī bhava
gate varṣasahasrānte rāmaṃ dṛṣṭvā yaśasvinam
tīrthayātrāprasaṅgena dhautapāpā bhaviṣyasi
evaṃ gate tataḥ kāle dṛṣṭā rāmeṇa dhīmatā
viśvāmitrasahāyena tyaktvā sāśmamayīṃ tanum
pūjayitvā yathānyāyaṃ gatapāpā vimatsarā
āgatā narmadātīre tīrthe snātvā yathāvidhi
kṛtaṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ māsaṃ kṛcchraṃ cānyaṃ tataḥ param
tatastuṣṭo mahādevo dattvā varamanuttamam
jagāmādarśanaṃ bhūyo reme comāpatiściram
ahalyā tu gate deve sthāpayitvā jagadgurum
ahalyeśvaranāmānaṃ svagṛhe cāgamatpunaḥ
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayet parameśvaram
sa mṛtaḥ svargamāpnoti yatra devo maheśvaraḥ
krīḍayitvā yathākāmaṃ tatra loke mahātapāḥ
gate varṣasahasrānte mānuṣyaṃ labhate punaḥ
dhanadhānyacayopetaḥ putrapautrasamanvitaḥ
vedavidyāśrayo dhīmāñjāyate vimale kule
rūpasaubhāgyasampannaḥ sarvavyādhivivarjitaḥ
jīvedvarṣaśataṃ sāgram ahalyātīrthasevanāt
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe ahalyātīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaṭtriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
dharmaputra tato gacchet karkaṭeśvaramuttamam
uttare narmadākūle sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram
tatra snātvā vidhānena yastu pūjayate śivam
anivartikā gatistasya rudralokād asaṃśayam
tasya tīrthasya māhātmyaṃ purāṇe yacchrutaṃ mayā
na tadvarṇayituṃ śakyaṃ saṃkṣepeṇa vadāmyataḥ
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ kuryātkiṃcitkarma śubhāśubham
harṣān madān mahārāja tatsarvaṃ jāyate 'kṣayam
tatra tīrthe tapastaptvā vālakhilyā marīcayaḥ
ramante 'dyāpi lokeṣu svecchayā kurunandana
tatrasthāstanna jānanti narājñānabahiṣkṛtāḥ
śarīrastham ivātmānam akṣayaṃ jyotikhyayam
tatra tīrthe nṛpaśreṣṭha devī nārāyaṇī purā
adyāpi tapate ghoraṃ tapo yāvatkilārbudam
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā tarpayet pitṛdevatāḥ
tasya te dvādaśābdāni tṛptiṃ yānti pitāmahāḥ
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe karkaṭeśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma saptatriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet pāṇḍuputra śakratīrtham anuttamam
yatra siddho mahābhāgo devarājaḥ śatakratuḥ
gautamena purā śaptaṃ jñātvā devāḥ sureśvaram
brahmādyā devatāḥ sarva ṛṣayaśca tapodhanāḥ
gautamaṃ prārthayāmāsur vākyaiḥ sānunayaiḥ śubhaiḥ
gatarājyaṃ gataśrīkaṃ śakraṃ prati munīśvara
indrena rahitaṃ rājyaṃ na kaścit kāmayed dvija
devo vā mānavo vāpi etatte viditaṃ prabho
tasya tvaṃ bhagayuktasya dayāṃ kuru dvijottama
gataścādarśanaṃ śakro dūṣitaḥ svena pāpmanā
devānāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā gautamo vedavittamaḥ
tatheti kṛtvā śakrasya varaṃ dātuṃ pracakrame
etadbhagasahasraṃ tu purā jātaṃ śatakrato
tallocanasahasraṃ tu matprasādād bhaviṣyati
evamuktaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ praṇamya munisattamam
brāhmaṇāṃs tān mahābhāgān narmadāṃ pratyagāt tataḥ
snātvā sa vimale toye saṃsthāpya tripurāntakam
jagāma tridaśāvāsaṃ pūjyamāno 'psarogaṇaiḥ
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayet parameśvaram
paradārābhigamanān mucyate pātakān naraḥ
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe śakratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanam nāmāṣṭatriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchen mahārāja somatīrthamanuttamam
yatra somastapastaptvā nakṣatrapathamāsthitaḥ
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snāyādācamya vidhipūrvakam
kṛtajāpyo raviṃ dhyāyet tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
ṛgvedayajurvedābhyāṃ sāmavedena bhārata
japato yatphalaṃ proktaṃ gāyatryā cātra tatphalam
tatra tīrthe tu yo bhaktyā brāhmaṇān bhojayecchuciḥ
tena samyagvidhānena koṭirbhavati bhojitā
pādukopānahau chatraṃ vastrakambalavājinaḥ
yo datte vipramukhyāya tasya tatkoṭisaṃmitam
sahasraṃ tu sahasrāṇāmanṛcāṃ yastu bhojayet
ekasya mantrayuktasya kalāṃ nārhati ṣoḍaśīm
evaṃ tu bhojayet tatra bahvṛcaṃ vedapāragam
śākhāntargam athādhvaryuṃ chandogaṃ vā samāptigam
agnihotrasahasrasya yatphalaṃ prāpyate budhaiḥ
samaṃ tadvedaviduṣā tīrthe somasya tatphalam
bhojayedyaḥ śataṃ teṣāṃ sahasraṃ labhate naraḥ
ekasya yogayuktasya tatphalaṃ kavayo viduḥ
saṃnirudhyendriyagrāmaṃ yatrayatra vasen muniḥ
tatratatra kurukṣetraṃ naimiṣaṃ puṣkarāṇi ca
tasmātsarvaprayatnena grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ
saṃkrāntau ca vyatīpāte yogī bhojyo viśeṣataḥ
saṃnyāsaṃ kurute yastu tatra tīrthe yudhiṣṭhira
vimānena mahābhāgāḥ sa yāti tridivaṃ naraḥ
somasyānucaro bhūtvā tenaiva saha modate
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe somatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikonacatvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahārāja nandāhradamanuttamam
yatra siddhā mahābhāgā nandā devī varapradā
mahiṣāsure mahākāye purā devabhayaṃkare
śūlinyā śūlabhinnāṅge kṛte dānavasattame
yenaikādaśarudrāśca hyādityāḥ samarudgaṇāḥ
vasavo vāyunā sārddhaṃ candrādityau sureśvara
balinā nirjitā yena brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ
saṅgrāme sumahāghore kṛte devabhayaṃkare
kṛtvā tatkadanaṃ ghoraṃ nandā devī sureśvarī
yasmātsnātā viśālākṣī tena nandāhradaḥ smṛtaḥ
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā nandāmuddiśya bhārata
dadāti dānaṃ viprebhyaḥ so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet
bhairavaṃ caiva kedāraṃ tathā rudraṃ mahālayam
nandāhradaścaturthaḥ syātpañcamaṃ bhuvi durlabham
bahavastaṃ na jānanti kāmarāgasamanvitāḥ
narmadāyā hradaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvapātakanāśanam
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā nandāṃ devīṃ prapūjayet
kiṃ tasya himavanmadhyagamanena prayojanam
paramārtham avijñāya paryaṭanti tamovṛtāḥ
teṣāṃ samāgame pārtha śrama eva hi kevalam
pṛthivyāṃ sāgarāntāyāṃ snānadānena yatphalam
tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti snātvā nandāhrade nṛpa
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe nandāhradatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma catvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchen mahīpāla tāpeśvaramanuttamam
yatra sā hariṇī siddhā vyādhabhītā nareśvara
jale prakṣipya gātrāṇi hyantarikṣaṃ gatā tu sā
vyādho vismitacittastu tāṃ mṛgīmavalokya ca
vimucya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ prārebhe tapa uttamam
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu vyādhenācaritaṃ tapaḥ
atīte tu tataḥ kāle parituṣṭo maheśvaraḥ
varaṃ brūhi mahāvyādha yatte manasi rocate
vyādha uvāca
yadi tuṣṭo 'si deveśa yadi deyo varo mama
tava pārśve mahādeva vāso me pratidīyatām
īśvara uvāca
evaṃ bhavatu te vyādha yastvayā kāṅkṣito varaḥ
daivadevo mahādeva ityuktvāntaradhīyata
gate cādarśanaṃ deve sthāpayitvā maheśvaram
pūjayitvā vidhānena gato vyādhastato divam
tadāprabhṛti tattīrthaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam
vyādhānutāpasaṃjātaṃ tāpeśvaramiti śrutam
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā sampūjayati śaṅkaram
śivalokamavāpnoti māmuvāca maheśvaraḥ
ye snātā narmadātoye tīrthe tāpeśvare narāḥ
tāpatrayavimuktāste nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ tṛtīyāyāṃ viśeṣataḥ
snānaṃ samācaren nityaṃ sarvapātakaśāntaye
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe tāpeśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikacatvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahārāja rukmiṇītīrthamuttamam
yatraiva snānamātreṇa rūpavānsubhago bhavet
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ tṛtīyāyāṃ viśeṣataḥ
snānaṃ samācaret tatra na ceha jāyate punaḥ
yaḥ snātvā rukmiṇītīrthe dānaṃ dadyāttu kāṃcanam
tattīrthasya prabhāvena śokaṃ nāpnoti mānavaḥ
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
tīrthasyāsya kathaṃ jāto mahimedṛṅmunīśvara
rūpasaubhāgyadaṃ yena tīrtham etad bravīhi me
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
kathayāmi yathāvṛttamitihāsaṃ purātanam
kathitaṃ pūrvato vṛddhaiḥ pāramparyeṇa bhārata
taṃ te 'haṃ sampravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvaikāgramānasaḥ
nagaraṃ kuṇḍinaṃ nāma bhīṣmakaḥ paripāti hi
hastyaśvarathasampanno dhanāḍhyo 'ti pratāpavān
strīsahasrasya madhyasthaḥ kurute rājyamuttamam
tasya bhāryā mahādevī prāṇebhyo 'pi garīyasī
tasyāmutpādayāmāsa putramekaṃ ca rukmakam
dvitīyā tanayā jajñe rukmiṇī nāma nāmataḥ
tadāśarīriṇī vācā rājānaṃ tamuvāca ha
caturbhujāya dātavyā kanyeyaṃ bhuvi bhīṣmaka
evaṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā jaharṣa priyayā saha
brāhmaṇaiḥ saha vidvadbhiḥ praviṣṭaḥ sūtikāgṛham
svastikaṃ vācayitvāsyāścakre nāmeti rukmiṇī
yataḥ suvarṇatilako janmanā saha bhārata
tataḥ sā rukmiṇīnāma brāhmaṇaiḥ kīrtitā tadā
tataḥ sā kālaparyāyādaṣṭavarṣā vyajāyata
pūrvoktaṃ caiva tadvākyamaśarīriṇyudīritam
smṛtvā smṛtvātha nṛpatiścintayāmāsa bhūpatiḥ
kasmai deyā mayā bālā bhavitā kaścaturbhujaḥ
etasminnantare tāvadraivatātparvatottamāt
mukhyaścedipatistatra damaghoṣaḥ samāgataḥ
praviṣṭo rājasadanaṃ yatra rājā sa bhīṣmakaḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā cāgataṃ gehe pūjayāmāsa bhūpatiḥ
āsanaṃ vipulaṃ dattvā sabhāṃ gatvā niveśitaḥ
kuśalaṃ tava rājendra damaghoṣa śriyāyuta
puṇyāhamadya saṃjātamahaṃ tvaddarśanotsukaḥ
kanyā madīyā rājendra hyaṣṭavarṣā vyajāyata
caturbhujāya dātavyā vāguvācāśarīriṇī
bhīṣmakasya vacaḥ śrutvā damaghoṣo 'bravīd idam
caturbhujo mama sutastriṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ
tasyeyaṃ dīyatāṃ kanyā śiśupālasya bhīṣmaka
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā damaghoṣasya bhūmipa
bhīṣmakena tato dattā śiśupālāya rukmiṇī
prārabdhaṃ maṅgalaṃ tatra bhīṣmakeṇa yudhiṣṭhira
dikṣu deśāntareṣveva ye vasanti svagotrajāḥ
nimantritāstu te sarve samājagmur yathākramam
tato yādavavaṃśasya tilakau balakeśavau
nimantritau samāyātau kuṇḍinaṃ bhīṣmakasya tu
bhīṣmakeṇa yathānyāyaṃ pūjitau tau yadūttamau
tataḥ pradoṣasamaye rukmiṇī kāmamohinī
sakhībhiḥ sahitā yātā pūrbahiścāmbikārcane
sāpaśyat tatra deveśaṃ gopaveṣadharaṃ harim
taṃ dṛṣṭvā mohamāpannā kāmena kaluṣīkṛtā
keśavo 'pi ca tāṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃkarṣaṇam uvāca ha
strīratnapravaraṃ tāta hartavyamiti me matiḥ
keśavasya vacaḥ śrutvā saṃkarṣaṇa uvāca ha
gaccha kṛṣṇa mahābāho strīratnaṃ cāśu gṛhyatām
ahaṃ ca tava mārgeṇa hyāgamiṣyāmi pṛṣṭhataḥ
dānavānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ kurvaṃśca kadanaṃ mahat
saṃkarṣaṇamataṃ prāpya keśavaḥ keśisūdanaḥ
yayau kanyāṃ gṛhītvā tu rathamāropya satvaram
nirgataḥ sahasā rājanvegenaivānilo yathā
hāhākāras tadā jāto bhīṣmakasya pure mahān
nirgatā dānavāḥ kruddhā velā iva mahodadheḥ
garjantaḥ sāyudhāḥ sarve dhāvanto rathavartmani
baladevaṃ tataḥ prāptā rathamārgānugāminam
teṣāṃ yuddhaṃ balasyāsīt sarvalokakṣayaṃkaram
yathā tārāmaye pūrvaṃ saṅgrāme lokaviśrute
gadāhasto mahābāhus trailokye 'pratimo balaḥ
halenākṛṣya sahasā gadāpātairapātayat
aśakyo dānavairhantuṃ balabhadro mahābalaḥ
babhañja dānavānsarvāṃstasthau giririvācalaḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā ca balaṃ kruddhaṃ durdharṣaṃ tridaśairapi
bhīṣmaputro mahātejā rukmīnām mahayaśāḥ
narāṇāmatiśūrāṇām akṣauhiṇyā samanvitaḥ
balabhadramatikramya tato yuddhe nirākarot
tadyuddhaṃ vañcayitvā tu rathamārgeṇa satvaram
keśavo 'pi tadā devo rukmiṇyā sahito yayau
vindhyaṃ tu laṅghayitvāgre trailokyagururavyayaḥ
narmadātaṭamāpede yatra siddhaḥ purā punaḥ
ajeyo yena saṃjātastīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ
etasmāt kāraṇāt tāta yodhanīpuram ucyate
rukmo 'pi dānavendro 'sau prāptaḥ
pratyuvācācyutaṃ kruddhas tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti mā vraja
adya tvāṃ niśitairbāṇairneṣyāmi yamasādanam
evaṃ parasparaṃ vīrau jagarjaturubhāvapi
tayoryuddhamabhūdghoraṃ tārakāgnijasannibham
cikṣepa śarajālāni keśavaṃ prati dānavaḥ
nānucintya śarāṃs tasya keśavaḥ keśisūdanaḥ
tato viṣṇuḥ svayaṃ kruddhaścakraṃ gṛhya sudarśanam
sampraharatyamuṃ yāvadrukmiṇyātra nivāritaḥ
tvāṃ na jānāti deveśaṃ caturbāhuṃ janārdanam
darśayasva svakaṃ rūpaṃ dayāṃ kṛtvā mamopari
evamuktastu rukmiṇyā darśayāmāsa bhārata
devā dṛṣṭvāpi tadrūpaṃ stuvantyākāśasaṃsthitāḥ
divyaṃ cakṣus tadā devo dadau rukmasya bhārata
rukma uvāca
yanmayā pāpaniṣṭhena mandabhāgyena keśava
sāyakairāhataṃ vakṣastatsarvaṃ kṣantumarhasi
pūrvaṃ dattā svayaṃ deva jānakī janakena vai
mayā pradattā deveśa rukmiṇī tava keśava
udvāhaya yathānyāyaṃ vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā
rukmasya vacanaṃ śrutvā tatastuṣṭo jagadguruḥ
babhāṣe devadeveśo rukmiṇaṃ bhīṣmakātmajam
gaccha svakaṃ puraṃ mā bhaiḥ kuru rājyamakaṇṭakam
keśavasya vacaḥ śrutvā rukmo dānavapuṃgavaḥ
taṃ praṇamya jagannāthaṃ jagāma bhavanaṃ pituḥ
gate rukme tadā kṛṣṇaḥ samāmantrya dvijottamān
marīcimatryaṅgirasaṃ pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum
vasiṣṭhaṃ ca mahābhāgamityete sapta mānasāḥ
ityete brāhmaṇāḥ sapta purāṇe niścayaṃ gatāḥ
kṣamāvantaḥ prajāvanto maharṣibhir alaṃkṛtāḥ
ityevaṃ brahmaputrāśca satyavanto mahāmate
narmadātaṭamāśritya nivasanti jitendriyāḥ
tapaḥsvādhyāyaniratā japahomaparāyaṇāḥ
nimantritāstu rājendra keśavena mahātmanā
śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ brahmoktavidhinā tataḥ
haristānpūjayāmāsa saptabrahmarṣipuṃgavān
pradadau dvādaśa grāmāṃstebhyastatra janārdanaḥ
yāvaccandraśca sūryaśca yāvattiṣṭhati medinī
tāvaddānaṃ mayā dattaṃ paripanthī na kaścana
maddattaṃ pālayiṣyante ye nṛpā gatakalmaṣāḥ
tebhyaḥ svasti kariṣyāmi dāsyāmi paramāṃ gatim
yāvaddhi yānti lokeṣu mahābhūtāni pañca ca
tāvatte divi modante maddattaparipālakāḥ
yastu lopayate mūḍho dattaṃ vaḥ pṛthivītale
narake tasya vāsaḥ syād yāvadābhūtasamplavam
svadattā paradattā vā pālanīyā vasuṃdharā
yasya yasya yadā bhūmis tasya tasya tadā phalam
svadattāṃ paradattāṃ vā yo hareta vasuṃdharām
sa viṣṭhāyāṃ kṛmirbhūtvā pitṛbhiḥ saha majjati
anyāyena hṛtā bhūmiranyāyena ca hāritā
hartā hārayitā caiva viṣṭhāyāṃ jāyate kṛmiḥ
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi svarge tiṣṭhati bhūmidaḥ
ācchettā cānumantā ca tānyeva narake vaset
yānīha dattāni purā narendrair dānāni dharmārthayaśaskarāṇi
nirmālyarūpapratimāni tāni ko nāma sādhuḥ punarādadāti
evaṃ tānpūjayitvā tu samyaṅ nyāyena pāṇḍava
rukmiṇyā vidhivatpāṇiṃ jagrāha madhusūdanaḥ
muśalī ca tataḥ sarvāñjitvā dānavapuṃgavān
svasthānam agamat tatra kṛtvā kāryaṃ suśobhanam
prayātau dvāravatyāṃ tau kṛṣṇasaṃkarṣaṇāvubhau
gacchamānaṃ tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā keśavaṃ kleśanāśanam
brāhmaṇāḥ satyavantaśca nirgatāḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ
āgacchamānāṃs tau vīkṣya rathamārgeṇa brāhmaṇān
muhūrtaṃ tatra viśramya keśavo vākyam abravīt
kimāgamanakāryaṃ vo brūta sarvaṃ dvijottamāḥ
kurvāṇāḥ svīyakarmāṇi mama kṛtyaṃ tu tiṣṭhate
devasya vacanaṃ śrutvā munayo vākyam abruvan
kalpakoṭisahasreṇa satyabhāvāttu vanditaḥ
duṣprāpyo 'si manuṣyāṇāṃ prāptaḥ kiṃ tyajase hi naḥ
brāhmaṇānāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā bhagavān idam abravīt
mathurāyāṃ dvāravatyāṃ yodhanīpura eva ca
trikālamāgamiṣyāmi satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
evaṃ te brāhmaṇāḥ śrutvā yodhanīpuramāgatāḥ
avatīrṇastribhāgena prādurbhāve tu māthure
etatte kathitaṃ sarvaṃ tīrthasyotpattikāraṇam
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyacca vartamānaṃ tathāparam
yaṃ śrutvā sarvapāpebhyo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayed balakeśavau
tena devo jagaddhātā pūjitastriguṇātmavān
upavāsī naro bhūtvā yastu kuryāt pradakṣiṇam
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
tatra tīrthe tu ye vṛkṣāstānpaśyantyapi ye narāḥ
te 'pi pāpaiḥ pramucyante bhrūṇahatyāsamair api
prātarutthāya ye kecitpaśyanti balakeśavau
tena te sadṛśāḥ syur vai devadevena cakriṇā
te pūjyāste namaskāryās teṣāṃ janma sujīvitam
ye namanti jagannāthaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim
tatra tīrthe tu yaddānaṃ snānaṃ devārcanaṃ nṛpa
tatsarvamakṣayaṃ tasya ityevaṃ śaṅkaro 'bravīt
praviśyāgnau mṛtānāṃ ca yatphalaṃ samudāhṛtam
tacchṛṇuṣva nṛpaśreṣṭha procyamānamaśeṣataḥ
vimānenārkavarṇena kiṃkiṇījālamālinā
āgneye bhavate tatra modate kālamīpsitam
jale caivā mṛtānāṃ tu yodhanīpuramadhyataḥ
vasanti vāruṇe loke yāvadābhūtasamplavam
anāśake mṛtānāṃ tu tatra tīrthe narādhipa
anivartikā gatir nṛṇāṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
tatra tīrthe tu yo dadyāt kapilādānamuttamam
vidhānena tu saṃyuktaṃ śṛṇu tasyāpi yatphalam
yāvanti tasyā romāṇi tatprasūteśca bhārata
tāvanti divi modante sarvakāmaiḥ supūjitāḥ
yāvanti romāṇi bhavanti dhenvāstāvanti varṣāṇi mahīyate saḥ
svargāc cyutaścāpi tatastrilokyāṃ kule samutpatsyati gomatāṃ saḥ
tatra tīrthe tu yo dadyād rūpyaṃ kāñcanameva vā
kāñcanena vimānena viṣṇuloke mahīyate
tasmiṃstīrthe tu yo dadyāt pāduke vastram eva ca
dānasyāsya prabhāvena labhate svargamīpsitam
ṛgyajuḥsāmavedānāṃ paṭhanād yatphalaṃ bhavet
tatra tīrthe tu rājendra gāyatryā tatphalaṃ labhet
prayāge yadbhavetpuṇyaṃ gayāyāṃ ca tripuṣkare
kurukṣetre tu rājendra rāhugraste divākare
someśvare ca yatpuṇyaṃ somasya grahaṇe tathā
tatphalaṃ labhate tatra snānamātrān na saṃśayaḥ
dvādaśyāṃ tu naraḥ snātvā namaskṛtya janārdanam
uddhṛtāḥ pitarastena avāptaṃ janmanaḥ phalam
saṃkrāntau ca vyatīpāte dvādaśyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ
brāhmaṇaṃ bhojayed ekaṃ koṭirbhavati bhojitā
pṛthivyāṃ yāni tīrthāni hyāsamudrāṇi pāṇḍava
tāni sarvāṇi tatraiva dvādaśyāṃ pāṇḍunandana
kṣayaṃ yānti ca dānāni yajñahomabalikriyāḥ
na kṣīyate mahārāja tatra tīrthe tu yatkṛtam
yadbhūtaṃ yadbhaviṣyacca tīrthamāhātmyamuttamam
kathitaṃ te mayā sarvaṃ pṛthagbhāvena bhārata
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe rukmiṇītīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma dvicatvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahārāja yojaneśvaram uttamam
yatra siddhau purā kalpe naranārāyaṇāvṛṣī
tatra tīrthe tapastaptvā saṅgrāme devadānavaiḥ
jayaṃ prāptau mahātmānau naranārāyaṇāvubhau
punastretāyuge prāpte tau devau rāmalakṣmaṇau
tatra tīrthe punaḥ snātvā rāvaṇo durjayo hataḥ
punaḥ pārtha kalau prāpte tau devau balakeśavau
vasudevakule jātau duṣkaraṃ karma cakratuḥ
narakaṃ kālanemiṃ ca kaṃsaṃ cāṇūramuṣṭikau
śiśupālaṃ jarāsaṃdhaṃ jaghnatur balakeśavau
tatastatra ripūnsaṃkhye bhīṣmadroṇapuraḥsarān
karṇaduryodhanādīṃśca nihaniṣyati sa prabhuḥ
dharmakṣetre kurukṣetre tatra yudhyanti te kṣaṇam
bhīmārjunanimittena śiṣyau kṛtvā parasparam
tatra tīrthe punargatvā tapaḥ kṛtvā suduṣkaram
pūjayitvā dvijānbhaktyā yāsyete dvārakāṃ punaḥ
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayed balakeśavau
tena devo jagaddhātā pūjitastriguṇātmavān
upavāsī naro bhūtvā yastu kuryāt prajāgaram
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo gāyaṃstasya śubhāṃ kathām
yāvatastatra tīrthe tu vṛkṣān paśyanti mānavāḥ
brahmahatyādikaṃ pāpaṃ tāvad eṣāṃ praṇaśyati
prātarutthāya ye kecit paśyanti balakeśavau
tenaiva sadṛśāḥ sarve devadevena cakriṇā
te pūjyāste namaskāryāsteṣāṃ janma sujīvitam
ye namanti jagatpūjyaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim
tatra tīrthe tu yaddānaṃ snānaṃ devārcanaṃ nṛpa
kriyate tatphalaṃ sarvamakṣayāyopakalpate
agnerapatyaṃ prathamaṃ suvarṇaṃ bhūrvaiṣṇavī sūryasutāśca gāvaḥ
lokāstrayastena bhavanti dattā yaḥ kāñcanaṃ gāṃ ca bhuvaṃ ca dadyāt
etatte kathitaṃ sarvaṃ tīrthamāhātmyamuttamam
atītaṃ ca bhaviṣyacca vartamānaṃ mahābalam
śrutvā vāpi paṭhitvedaṃ śrāvayipatvātha dhārmikān
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe yojaneśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma tricatvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahārāja dvādaśītīrthamuttamam
kṣaranti sarvadānāni japahomabalikriyāḥ
na kṣīyate tu rājendra cakratīrthe tu yatkṛtam
yadbhūtaṃ yadbhaviṣyacca tīrthamāhātmyamuttamam
kathitaṃ tanmayā sarvaṃ pṛthagbhāvena bhārata
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe dvādaśītīrthamahātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma catuścatvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gaccheddharāpāla śīvatīrthamanuttamam
darśanādyasya devasya mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ
śivatīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā jitakrodho jitendriyaḥ
pūjayeta mahādevaṃ so 'gniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet
tatra tīrthe tu yo bhaktyā sopavāso 'rcayecchivam
anivartikā gatistasya rudralokād asaṃśayam
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe śivatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma pañcacatvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
asmāhakaṃ tato gacchet pitṛtīrthamanuttamam
pretatvādyatra mucyante piṇḍenaikena pūrvajāḥ
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
asmāhakasya māhātmyaṃ kathayasva mamānagha
snānadānena yatpuṇyaṃ tathā piṇḍodakena ca
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
purā kalpe nṛpaśreṣṭha ṛṣidevasamāgame
praśnaḥ pṛṣṭo mayā tāta yathā tvamanupṛcchasi
ekatra sāgarāḥ sapta saprayāgāḥ sapuṣkarāḥ
nāsya sāmyaṃ labhante te nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
somanāthaṃ tu vikhyātaṃ yatsomena pratiṣṭhitam
tatra somagrahe puṇyaṃ tatpuṇyaṃ labhate naraḥ
māsānte pitaro nṛṇāṃ vīkṣante santatiṃ svakām
kaścid asmatkule 'smākaṃ piṇḍamatra pradāsyati
prapitāmahāstathādityāḥ śrutireṣā sanātanī
evaṃ bruvanti devāśca ṛṣayaḥ satapodhanāḥ
sakṛtpiṇḍodakenaiva śṛṇu pārthiva yatphalam
dvādaśābdāni rājendra yogaṃ bhuktvā suśobhanam
yuge yuge mahārāja asmāhake pitāmahāḥ
sarvadā hyavalokanta āgacchantaṃ svagotrajam
bhaviṣyati kim asmākam amāvāsyāpyamāhake
snānaṃ dānaṃ ca ye kuryuḥ pitṝṇāṃ tilatarpaṇam
te sarvapāpanirmuktāḥ sarvānkāmāṃllabhati vai
jalamadhye 'tra bhūpāla agnitīrthaṃ ca tiṣṭhati
darśanāt tasya tīrthasya pāparāśirvilīyate
snānamātreṇa rājendra brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati
śuklāmbaradharo nityaṃ niyataḥ sa jitendriyaḥ
ekakālaṃ tu bhuñjāno māsaṃ tīrthasya sannidhau
suvarṇālaṃkṛtānāṃ tu kanyānāṃ śatadānajam
phalamāpnoti sampūrṇaṃ pitṛloke mahīyate
pṛthivyām āsamudrāyāṃ mahābhogapatirbhavet
dhanadhānyasamāyukto dātā bhavati dhārmikaḥ
upavāsī śucirbhūtvā brahmalokamavāpnuyāt
asmāhakaṃ samāsādya yastu prāṇān parityajet
koṭivarṣasahasrāṇi rudraloke mahīyate
tataḥ svargāt paribhraṣṭaḥ kṣīṇakarmā divaścyutaḥ
suvarṇamaṇimuktāḍhye kule jāyeta rūpavān
kṛtvābhiṣekavidhinā hayamedhaphalaṃ labhet
dhanāḍhyo rūpavāndakṣo dātā bhavati dhārmikaḥ
caturvedeṣu yatpuṇyaṃ satyavādiṣu yatphalam
tatphalaṃ labhate nūnaṃ tatra tīrthe 'bhiṣecanāt
tīrthānāṃ paramaṃ tīrthaṃ nirmitaṃ śambhunā purā
hṛdayeśaḥ svayaṃ viṣṇur japeddevaṃ maheśvaram
gandharvāpsarasaścaiva maruto mārutāstathā
viśvedevāśca pitaraḥ sacandrāḥ sadivākarāḥ
marīciratryaṅgirasau pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ
pracetāśca vasiṣṭhaśca bhṛgurnārada eva ca
cyavano gālavaścaiva vāmadevo mahāmuniḥ
vālakhilyāśca gandhārāstṛṇabinduśca jājaliḥ
uddālakaścarṣyaśṛṅgo vasiṣṭhaśca sanandanaḥ
śukraścaiva bharadvājo vātsyo vātsyāyanastathā
agastirmitrāvaruṇau viśvāmitro munīśvaraḥ
gautamaśca pulastyaśca paulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ
sanātanastu kapilo vāhniḥ pañcaśikhastathā
anye 'pi bahavastatra munayaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ
krīḍanti devatāḥ sarva ṛṣayaḥ satapodhanāḥ
manuṣyāścaiva yogīndrāḥ pitaraḥ sapitāmahāḥ
asmāhake 'tra tiṣṭhanti sarva eva na saṃśayaḥ
pitaraḥ pitāmahāścaiva tathaiva prapitāmahāḥ
yeṣāṃ dattamupasthāyi sukṛtaṃ vāpi duṣkṛtam
akṣayaṃ tatra tatsarvaṃ yatkṛtaṃ yodhanīpure
mātaraṃ pitaraṃ tyaktvā sarvabandhusuhṛjjanān
dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ priyānputrāṃs tathā dehaṃ nṛpottama
gacchate vāyubhūtastu śubhāśubhasamanvitaḥ
adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ paramātmā mahattaraḥ
śubhāśubhagatiṃ prāptaḥ karmaṇā svena pārthiva
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
śubhāśubhaṃ na bandhūnāṃ jāyate kena hetunā
ekaḥ prasūyate jantureka eva pralīyate
eko hi bhuṅkte sukṛtameka eva hi duṣkṛtam
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
eṣa tvayokto nṛpate mahāpraśnaḥ smṛto mayā
pitāmahamukhodgītaṃ śrutaṃ te kathayāmyaham
yanme pitāmahātpūrvaṃ vijñātam ṛṣisaṃsadi
na mātā na pitā bandhuḥ kasyacinna suhṛtkvacit
kasya na jñāyate rūpaṃ vāyubhūtasya dehinaḥ
yadyevaṃ na bhavettāta lokasya tu nareśvara
amaryādaṃ bhavennūnaṃ vinaśyati carācaram
evaṃ jñātvā pūrā rājansamastairlokakartṛbhiḥ
maryādā sthāpitā loke yathā dharmo na naśyati
dharme naṣṭe manuṣyāṇām adharmo 'bhibhavet punaḥ
tataḥ svadharmacalanānnarake gamanaṃ dhruvam
loko niraṅkuśaḥ sarvo maryādālaṅghane rataḥ
maryādā sthāpitā tena śāstraṃ vīkṣya maharṣibhiḥ
snānaṃ dānaṃ japo homaḥ svādhyāyo devatārcanam
piṇḍodakapradānaṃ ca tathaivātithipūjanam
pitaraḥ pitāmahāścaiva tathaiva prapitāmahāḥ
trayo devāḥ smṛtāstāta brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ
pūjitaiḥ pūjitāḥ sarve tathā mātāmahāstrayaḥ
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena śrutismṛtyarthanoditān
dharmaṃ samācarannityaṃ pāpāṃśena na lipyate
śrutismṛtyuditaṃ dharmaṃ manasāpi na laṅghayet
iha loke pare caiva yadīcchecchreya ātmanaḥ
pitāputrau sadāpyekau bimbādbimbamivoddhṛtau
vibhaktau vāvibhaktau vā śrutismṛtyarthatastathā
uddharedātmanātmānam ātmānam avasādayet
piṇḍodakapradānābhyāmṛte pārtha na saṃśayaḥ
evaṃ jñātvā prayatnena piṇḍodakaprado bhavet
āyurdharmo yaśastejaḥ santatiścaiva vardhate
pṛthivyāṃ sāgarāntāyāṃ pitṛkṣetrāṇi yāni ca
tāni te sampravakṣyāmi yeṣu dattaṃ mahāphalam
gayāyāṃ puṣkare jyeṣṭhe prayāge naimiṣe tathā
saṃnihatyāṃ kurukṣetre prabhāse kurunandana
piṇḍodakapradānena yatphalaṃ kathitaṃ budhaiḥ
asmāhake tadāpnoti narmadāyāṃ na saṃśayaḥ
tatra brahmā murāriśca rudraśca umayā saha
indrādyā devatāḥ sarve pitaro munayastathā
sāgarāḥ saritaścaiva parvatāśca balāhakāḥ
tiṣṭhanti pitaraḥ sarve sarvatīrthādhikaṃ tataḥ
sthitā brahmaśilā tatra gajakumbhanibhā nṛpa
kalau na dṛśyā bhavati pradhānaṃ yadgayāśiraḥ
vaiśākhe māsi samprāpte 'māvāsyāṃ nṛpottama
vyāpya sā tiṣṭhate tīrthaṃ gajakumbhanibhā śilā
tacca gavyūtimātraṃ hi tīrthaṃ tataḥ pravakṣate
tasmindine tatra gatvā yastu śrāddhaprado bhavet
pitṝṇām akṣayā tṛptirjāyate śatavārṣikī
anyasyāmapyamāvāsyāṃ yaḥ snātvā vijitendriyaḥ
karoti manujaḥ śrāddhaṃ vidhivanmantrasaṃyutam
tasya puṇyaphalaṃ yatsyāt tacchṛṇuṣva narādhipa
agniṣṭomāśvamedhābhyāṃ vājapeyasya yatphalam
tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti yathā me śaṅkaro 'bravīt
rauravādiṣu sarveṣu narakeṣu vyavasthitāḥ
pitā pitāmahādyāśca pitṛke mātṛke tathā
piṇḍodakena caikena tarpaṇena viśeṣataḥ
krīḍanti pitṛlokasthā yāvad ābhūtasamplavam
ye karmasthā vikarmasthā ye jātāḥ pretakalmaṣāḥ
piṇḍenaikena mucyante te 'pi tatra na saṃśayaḥ
asmāhake śilā divyā tiṣṭhate gajasannibhā
brahmaṇā nirmitā pūrvaṃ sarvapāpakṣayaṃkarī
uparyasyā yathānyāyaṃ pitṝn uddiśya bhārata
dakṣiṇāgreṣu darbheṣu dadyātpiṇḍānvicakṣaṇaḥ
bhūmau cānnena siddhena śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi
śrāddhibhyo vastrayugmāni chatropānatkamaṇḍalu
dakṣiṇā vividhā deyā pitṝn uddiśya bhārata
yo dadāti dvijaśreṣṭha tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
tasya te dvādaśābdāni tṛptiṃ yānti na saṃśayaḥ
asmāhake mahārāja pitaraśca pitāmahāḥ
vāyubhūtā nirīkṣante āgacchantaṃ svagotrajam
atra tīrthe suto 'bhyetya snātvā toyaṃ pradāsyati
śrāddhaṃ vā piṇḍadānaṃ vā tena yāsyāma sadgatim
snāne kṛte tu ye kecij jāyante vastravipluṣaḥ
prīṇayennarakasthāṃstu taiḥ pitṝn nātra saṃśayaḥ
keśodabindavas tasya ye cānye lepabhājinaḥ
tṛpyantyanagninasaṃskārā yaṃ mṛtāḥ syuḥ svagotrajāḥ
tatra tīrthe tu ye kecic chrāddhaṃ kṛtvā vidhānataḥ
narakāduddharantyāśu japantaḥ pitṛsaṃhitām
vanaspatigate some yadā somadinaṃ bhavet
akṣayāllabhate lokānpiṇḍenaikena mānavaḥ
akṣayaṃ tatra vai sarvaṃ jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
narakāduddharantyāśu japante pitṛsaṃhitām
tasmiṃstīrthe tvamāvāsyāṃ pitṝn uddiśya bhārata
nīlaṃ sarvāṅgasampūrṇaṃ yo 'bhiṣicya samutsṛjet
tasya puṇyaphalaṃ vaktuṃ na tu vācaspatiḥ kṣamaḥ
asmāhake vṛṣotsargādyatpuṇyaṃ samavāpyate
tava śuśrūṣaṇāt sarvaṃ tatpravakṣyāmi bhārata
rauravādiṣu ye kiṃcit pacyante tasya pūrvajāḥ
vṛṣotsargeṇa tānsarvāṃstārayedekaviṃśatim
lohito yastu varṇena mukhe pucche ca pāṇḍuraḥ
piṅgaḥ khuraviṣāṇābhyāṃ sa nīlo vṛṣa ucyate
yastu sarvāṅgapiṅgaśca śvetaḥ pucchakhureṣu ca
sa piṅgo vṛṣa ityāhuḥ pitṝṇāṃ prītivardhanaḥ
pārāvatasavarṇaśca lalāṭe tilako bhavet
taṃ vṛṣaṃ babhrumityāhuḥ pūrṇaṃ sarvāṅgaśobhanam
sarvāṅgeṣv ekavarṇo yaḥ piṅgaḥ pucchakhureṣu ca
khurapiṅgaṃ tamityāhuḥ pitṝṇāṃ sadgatipradam
nīlaṃ sarvaśarīreṇa svāraktanayanaṃ dṛḍham
tameva nīlamityāhurnīlaḥ pañcavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ
yastu vaiśyagṛhe jātaḥ sa vai nīlo viśiṣyate
na vāhayedgṛhe jātaṃ vatsakaṃ tu kadācana
tenaiva ca vṛṣotsarge pitṝṇām anṛṇo bhavet
jātaṃ tu svagṛhe vatsaṃ dvijanmā yastu vāhayet
patanti pitarastasya brahmakokagatā api
yathāyathā hi pibati pītvā dhūnāti mastakam
pibanpitṝn prīṇayati narakāduddhared dhunan
yathā pucchābhighātena skandhaṃ gacchanti bindavaḥ
narakāduddharantyāśu patitān gotriṇas tathā
garjanprāvṛṣi kāle tu viṣāṇābhyāṃ bhuvaṃ likhan
khurebhyo yā mṛdudbhūtā tayā saṃprīṇayed ṛṣīn
pibanpitṝn prīṇayate khādanollekhane surān
garjannṛṣimanuṣyāṃśca dharmarūpo hi dharmaja
bhūtairvāpi piśācairvā cāturthikajvareṇa vā
gṛhīto 'smāhakaṃ gacchet sarveṣām ādhināśanam
snātvā tu vimale toye darbhagranthiṃ nibandhayet
mastake bāhumūle vā nābhyāṃ vā galake 'pi vā
gatvā devasamīpaṃ ca prādakṣiṇyena keśavam
tataḥ samuccaran mantraṃ gāyatryā vātha vaiṣṇavam
nārāyaṇaṃ śaraṇyeśaṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam
namo yajñāṅgasambhūta sarvavyāpinnamo 'stu te
namo namaste deveśa padmagarbha sanātana
dāmodara jayānanta rakṣa māṃ śaraṇāgatam
tvaṃ kartā tvaṃ ca hartā ca jagat yasmiṃścarācare
tvaṃ pālayasi bhūtāni bhuvanaṃ tvaṃ bibharṣi ca
prasīda devadeveśa suptamaṅgaṃ prabodhaya
tvaddhyānanirato nityaṃ tvadbhaktiparamo hare
iti stuto mayā deva prasādaṃ kuru me 'cyuta
māṃ rakṣa rakṣa pāpebhyastrāyasva śaraṇāgatam
evaṃ stutvā ca deveśaṃ dānavāntakaraṃ harim
punaruktena vai snātvā tato viprāṃstu bhojayet
vedoktena vidhānena snānaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi
piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ kṛtvā vācayetsvastikaṃ tataḥ
evaṃ stutvā ca deveśaṃ dānavāntakaraṃ harim
punaruktena vai snātvā tato viprāṃstu bhojayet
vedoktena vidhānena snānaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi
evaṃ tānvācayitvā tu tato viprānvisarjayet
yattatroccaritaṃ kiṃcittadviprebhyo nivedayet
tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā nārī vā bhaktitatparā
śaktito dakṣiṇāṃ dadyātkṛtvā śrāddhaṃ yathāvidhi
tatra tīrthe naro yāvat snāpayed vidhipūrvakam
kṣīreṇa madhunā vāpi dadhnā vā śītavāriṇā
tāvatpuṣkarapātreṣu pibanti pitaro jalam
ayane viṣuve caiva yugādau sūryasaṃkrame
puṣpaiḥ sampūjya deveśaṃ naivedyaṃ yaḥ pradāpayet
so 'śvamedhasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoti puṣkalam
tatra tīrthe tu yo rājan sūryagrahaṇam ācaret
sūryatejonibhairyānairviṣṇuloke mahīyate
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ śrāddhaṃ pitṛbhyaḥ samprayacchati
satputreṇa ca tenaiva samprāptaṃ janmanaḥ phalam
iti śrutvā tato devāḥ sarve śakrapurogamāḥ
brahmaviṣṇumaheśāśca sthāpayāṃcakrur īśvaram
sarvarogopaśamanaṃ sarvapātakanāśanam
yastu saṃvatsaraṃ pūrṇamamāvāsyāṃ tu bhāvitaḥ
pitṛbhyaḥ piṇḍadānaṃ ca kuryādasmāhake nṛpa
tripuṣkare gayāyāṃ ca prabhāse naimiṣe tathā
yatpuṇyaṃ śrāddhakartṝṇāṃ tadihaiva bhaveddhruvam
tilodakaṃ kuśairmiśraṃ yo dadyāddakṣiṇāmukhaḥ
manvādau ca yugādau ca vyatīpāte dinakṣaye
yo dadyāt pitṛmātṛbhyaḥ so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet
asmāhake naro yastu snātvā sampūjayeddharim
brahmāṇaṃ śaṅkaraṃ bhaktyā kuryāj jāgaraṇakriyām
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ śakrātithyamavāpnuyāt
tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā yaḥ paśyati janārdanam
viśeṣavidhinābhyarcya praṇamya ca punaḥpunaḥ
saputreṇa ca tenaiva pitṝṇāṃ vihitā gatiḥ
ekamūrtistrayo devā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ
satkāryakāraṇopetāḥ susūkṣmāḥ sumahāphalāḥ
etatte kathitaṃ rājanmahāpātakanāśanam
asmāhakasya māhātmyaṃ kimanyat paripṛcchasi
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe asmāhakatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaṭcatvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahīpāla siddheśvaramanuttamam
narmadādakṣiṇe kūle tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayed vṛṣabhadhvajam
sarvapāpavinirmukto gatiṃ yātyaśvamedhinām
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā śrāddhaṃ kuryāt prayatnataḥ
pitṝṇāṃ prīṇanārthāya sarvaṃ tena kṛtaṃ bhavet
tatra tīrthe mṛtānāṃ tu jantūnāṃ nṛpasattama
garbhavāse matisteṣāṃ na jāyeta kadācana
garbhavāso hi duḥkhāya na sukhāya kadācana
tattīrthavāriṇā snātur na punarbhavasambhavaḥ
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe siddheśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma saptacatvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahīpāla tīrthamaṅgārakaṃ śivam
uttare narmadākūle sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram
caturthyaṅgārakadine saṃkalpya kṛtaniścayaḥ
snāyādastaṃ gate sūrye sandhyopāsanatatparaḥ
pūjayellohitaṃ bhaktyā gandhamālyavibhūṣaṇaiḥ
saṃsthāpyasthaṇḍile devaṃ raktacandanacarcitam
