iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe aṣāḍhītīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma ṣoḍaśottaradviśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
eraṇḍīsaṅgamaṃ gacchet surāsuranamaskṛtam
tattu tīrthaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam
upavāsaparo bhūtvā niyatendriyamānasaḥ
tatra snātvā vidhānena mucyate brahmahatyayā
tatra tīrthe tu yo bhaktyā prāṇatyāgaparo bhavet
anivartikā gatis tasya rudralokād asaṃśayam
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe eraṇḍītīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma saptadaśottaradviśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gaccheddharādhīśa tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam
jamadagniriti khyātaṃ yatra siddho janārdanaḥ
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kathaṃ siddho dvijaśreṣṭha vāsudevo jagadguruḥ
mānuṣaṃ rūpamāsthāya lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
etatsarvaṃ yathānyāyaṃ devadevasya cakriṇaḥ
caritaṃ śrotum icchāmi kathyamānaṃ tvayānagha
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
āsītpūrvaṃ mahārāja haihayādhipatirmahān
kārtavīrya iti khyāto rājā bāhusahasravān
hastyaśvarathasampannaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
vedavidyāvratasnātaḥ sarvabhūtābhayapradaḥ
māhiṣmatyāḥ patiḥ śrīmānrājā hyakṣauhiṇīpatiḥ
sa kadācinmṛgānhantuṃ nirjagāma mahābalaḥ
bahubhir divasaiḥ prāpto bhṛgukacchamanuttamam
jamadagnir mahātejā yatra tiṣṭhati tāpasaḥ
reṇukāsahitaḥ śrīmānsarvabhūtābhayapradaḥ
tasya putro 'bhavadrāmaḥ sākṣānnārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ
sarvakṣatraguṇairyukto brahmavidbrāhmaṇottamaḥ
toṣayanparayā bhaktyā pitarau paramārthavat
taṃ tadā cārjunaṃ dṛṣṭvā jamadagniḥ pratāpavān
carantaṃ mṛgayāṃ gatvā hyātithyena nyamantrayat
tatheti coktvā sa nṛpaḥ sabhṛtyabalavāhanaḥ
jagāma cāśramaṃ puṇyamṛṣestasya mahātmanaḥ
tatkṣaṇād eva sampannaṃ śriyā paramayā vṛtam
vismayaṃ paramaṃ tatra dṛṣṭvā rājā jagāma ha
gatamātrastu siddhena paramānnena bhojitaḥ
sabhṛtyabalavānrājā brāhmaṇena yadṛcchayā
kimetad iti papraccha kāraṇaṃ śaktimeva ca
kāmadhenoḥ prabhāvaṃ taṃ jñātvā prāha tato dvijam
dakṣiṇāṃ dehi me vipra kalmaṣāṃ dhenumuttamām
śataṃ śatasahasrāṇām ayutaṃ niyutaṃ param
bhūṣitānāṃ ca dhenūnāṃ dadāmi tava cārbudam
jamadagnir uvāca
ayutaiḥ prayutair nāhaṃ śatakoṭibhiruttamām
kāmadhenumimāṃ tāta na dadmi pratigamyatām
evamuktaḥ sa rājendras tena vipreṇa bhārata
krodhasaṃraktanayana idaṃ vacanamabravīt
yasyedṛśaḥ kāmacāro mayyapi dvijapāṃsana
ahaṃ te paśyatastasmānnayāmi surabhiṃ gṛhāt
dvija uvāca
kaḥ krīḍati saroṣeṇa nirbhayo hi mahāhinā
mṛtyudṛṣṭotareṇāpi mama dhenuṃ nayeta yaḥ
evamuktvā mahādaṇḍaṃ brahmadaṇḍamivāparam
gṛhītvā paramakruddho jamadagniruvāca ha
yasyāsti śaktistejo vā kṣatriyasya kulādhamaḥ
dhenuṃ nayatu me sadyaḥ kṣīṇāyuḥ saparicchadaḥ
etacchrutvā vacaḥ krūraṃ haihayaḥ śataśo vṛtaḥ
dhāvamānaḥ kṣititale brahmadaṇḍahato 'patat
huṃkṛtena tato dhenvāḥ khaḍgapāśāsipāṇayaḥ
nirgacchantaḥ pradṛśyante kalmaṣāyāḥ sahasraśaḥ
nāsāpuṭāgrādromāgrātkirātā māgadhā gudāt
randhrāntareṣu cotpannāḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
evamanyo 'nyamāhatya haihayaṣṭaṅkaṇāndahan
vināśaṃ saha vipreṇa gatā hyarjunatejasā
kārtavīryo jayaṃ labdhvā saṃkhye hatvā dvijottamam
jagāma svāṃ purīṃ hṛṣṭaḥ kṛtāntavaśamohitaḥ
tatastvarānvitaḥ prāptaḥ paścādrāmo gate ripau
ākrandamānāṃ jananīṃ dadarśa piturantike
rāma uvāca
kenedamātmanāśāya hyajñānāt sāhasaṃ kṛtam
mama tātaṃ jighāṃsuryo draṣṭuṃ mṛtyumihecchati
tataḥ sā rāmavākyena gatasattveva vihvalā
udaraṃ karayugmena tāḍayantī hyuvāca tam
arjunena nṛśaṃsena kṣatriyair aparaiḥ saha
ihāgatya pitā tena nihato bāhuśālinā
taṃ paśya nihataṃ tātaṃ gatāsuṃ gatacetasam
saṃskṛtya vidhivatputra tarpayasva yathātatham
etacchrutvā sa vacanaṃ jananīm abhivādya tām
pratijñām akarod yāṃ tāṃ śṛṇuṣva ca narādhipa
triḥsaptakṛtvaḥ pṛthivīṃ niḥkṣatriyakulānvayām
snātvā ca teṣām asṛjā tarpayiṣyāmi te patim
tasyāpi paraśunā bāhūn kārtavīryasya durmateḥ
chittvā pāsyāmi rudhiramiti satyaṃ śṛṇuṣva me
evaṃ pratijñāṃ kṛtvāsau jāmadagnyaḥ pratāpavān
krodhena mahatāviṣṭaḥ saṃskṛtya pitaraṃ tataḥ
māhiṣmatīṃ purīṃ rāmo jagāma krodhamūrchitaḥ
chittvā bāhuvanaṃ tasya hatvā taṃ kṣatriyādhamam
jagāma kṣatriyāntāya pṛthivīm avalokayan
saptadvīpārṇavayutāṃ saśailavanakānanām
pūrvataḥ paścimāmāśāṃ dakṣiṇottarataḥ kurūn
samantapañcake pañca cakāra rudhirahradān
sa teṣu rudhirāmbhastu hradeṣu krodhamūrchitaḥ
pitṝn saṃtarpayāmāsa rudhireṇeti naḥ śrutam
atharcīkādaya upetya pitaro brāhmaṇarṣabham
taṃ kṣamasveti jagadus tataḥ sa virarāma ha
teṣāṃ samīpe yo deśo hradānāṃ rudhirāmbhasām
samaṃ tapaṃ cakram iti puṇyaṃ tatparikīrtitam
nivartya karmaṇastasmāt pitṝn provāca pāṇḍava
rāmaḥ paramadharmātmā yadidaṃ rudhiraṃ mayā
kṣiptaṃ pañcasu tīrtheṣu tadbhūyāt tīrthamuttamam
tathetyuktvā tu te sarve pitaro 'dṛśyatāṃ gatāḥ
evaṃ rāmasya saṃsargo devamārge yudhiṣṭhira
sarvapāpakṣayakaro darśanātsparśanān nṛṇām
reṇukāpratyayārthāya adyāpi pitṛdevatāḥ
dṛśyante devamārgasthāḥ sarvapāpakṣayaṃkarāḥ
tatra tīrthe tu rājendra narmadodadhisaṅgame
sthānaṃ kṛtvā vidhānena mucyante pātakairnarāḥ
kuśāgreṇāpi kaunteya na spṛṣṭavyo mahodadhiḥ
anena tatra mantreṇa snātavyaṃ nṛpasattama
namaste viṣṇurūpāya namastubhyam apāṃ pate
sānnidhyaṃ kuru deveśa sāgare lavaṇāmbhasi
iti sparśanamantraḥ
agniśca tejo mṛḍayā ca dehe reto 'tha viṣṇuramṛtasya nābhiḥ
etad bruvan pāṇḍava satyavākyaṃ tato 'vagāheta patiṃ nadīnām
pañcaratnasamāyuktaṃ phalapuṣpākṣatairyutam
mantreṇānena rājendra dadyādarghaṃ mahodadheḥ
sarvaratnanidhānastvaṃ sarvaratnākarākaraḥ
sarvāmarapradhāneśa gṛhāṇārghaṃ namo 'stu te
ityarghamantraḥ
ā janmajanitāt pāpānmāmuddhara mahodadhe
yāhyarcito ratnanidhe parvatān pārvaṇottama
iti visarjanamantraḥ
ko 'paraḥ sāgarāddevātsvargadvāravipāṭana
tatra sāgaraparyantaṃ mahātīrthamanuttamam
jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa tatra devaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ
yatra devāḥ sagandharvā munayaḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ
upāsate virūpākṣaṃ jamadagnim anuttamam
reṇukāṃ caiva ye devīṃ paśyanti bhuvi mānavāḥ
priyavāse śive loke vasanti kālamīpsitam
tatra snātvā naro rājaṃstarpayanpitṛdevatāḥ
tārayen narakādghorāt kulānāṃ śatamuttaram
snātvā dattvātra sahitāḥ śrutvā vai bhaktipūrvakam
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe jāmadagnyatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭādaśādhikadviśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
narmadādakṣiṇe kūle tīrthaṃ koṭīśvaraṃ param
yatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca sarvaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet
tatra devāḥ sagandharvā ṛṣayo ye tathāmalāḥ
koṭitīrthe parāṃ siddhiṃ samprāptā bhuvi durlabhām
sthāpitaśca mahādevastatra koṭīśvaro nṛpa
taṃ dṛṣṭvā devadeveśaṃ siddhiṃ prāpnotyanuttamām
tatra tīrthe tu yatkiṃcicchubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham
kriyate tannṛpaśreṣṭha sarvaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet
tatra dakṣiṇamārgasthā ye kecinmunisattamāḥ
siddhā mṛtāḥ padaṃ yānti pitṛlokaṃ dhruvaṃ hi te
uttaraṃ narmadākūlaṃ ye śreṣṭhā munipuṃgavāḥ
devalokaṃ gatāḥ pūrvamiti śāstrasya niścayaḥ
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe koṭitīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikonaviṃśadadhikadviśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gaccheddharādhīśa loṭaṇeśvaram uttamam
uttare narmadākūle sarvapātakanāśanam
tatkṣaṇādeva tatsarvaṃ saptajanmārjitaṃ tvagham
naśyate devadevasya darśanādeva tannṛpa
bālyātprabhṛti yatpāpaṃ yauvane cāpi yatkṛtam
tatsarvaṃ vilayaṃ yāti devadevasya darśanāt
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
āścaryabhūtaṃ lokeṣu narmadācaritaṃ mahat
tvayā vai kathitaṃ vipra sakalaṃ pāpanāśanam
yadekaṃ paramaṃ tīrthaṃ sarvatīrthaphalapradam
śrotumicchāmi tatsarvaṃ dayāṃ kṛtvā vadāśu me
ye kecid durlabhāḥ praśnāstriṣu lokeṣu sattama
tvatprasādena te sarve śrutā me saha bāndhavaiḥ
etamekaṃ paraṃ praśnaṃ sarvapraśnavidāṃ vara
śrutvāhaṃ tvatprasādena yatra yāmi sabāndhavaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
sādhusādhu mahāprājña yasya te matirīdṛśī
durlabhaṃ triṣu lokeṣu tasya te nāsti kiṃcana
dharmamarthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca mokṣaṃ ca bharatarṣabha
kāle kāle ca yo vetti kartavyas tena dhīmatā
tasmāt te sampravakṣyāmi praśnasyāsyottaraṃ śubham
yacchrutvā sarvapāpebhyo mucyante bhuvi mānavāḥ
narmadā saritāṃ śreṣṭhā sarvatīrthamayī śubhā
viśeṣaḥ kathitastasyā revāsāgarasaṅgame
āgacchantīṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha dṛṣṭvā revāṃ mahodadhiḥ
praṇamya ca punardevīṃ saṅgame revayā saha
saṃcintya manasā keyamiti māṃ vai saridvarā
jñātvā saṃcintya manasā revāṃ liṅgodbhavāṃ parām
luṭhanvai sammukhastāta gato revāṃ mahodadhiḥ
samudre narmadā yatra praviṣṭāsti mahānadī
tatra devādhidevasya samudre liṅgamutthitam
liṅgodbhūtā mahābhāgā narmadā saritāṃ varā
layaṃ gatā tatra liṅge tena puṇyatamā hi sā
narmadāyāṃ vasannityaṃ narmadāmbu pibansadā
dīkṣitaḥ sarvayajñeṣu somapānaṃ dine dine
saṅgame tatra yaḥ snātvā loṭaṇeśvaram arcayet
so 'śvamedhasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ
vācikaṃ mānasaṃ pāpaṃ karmaṇā yatkṛtaṃ nṛpa
loṭaṇeśvaram āsādya sarvaṃ vilayatāṃ vrajet
kārttikyāṃ tu viśeṣeṇa kathitaṃ śaṅkareṇa tu
tacchṛṇuṣva nṛpaśreṣṭha sarvapāpāpanodanam
samprāptāṃ kārttikīṃ dṛṣṭvā gatvā tatra nṛpottama
caturdaśyāmupoṣyaiva snātvā vai narmadājale
saṃtarpya pitṛdevāṃśca śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi
rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ kuryātsampūjya loṭaṇeśvaram
saphalaṃ jīvitaṃ tasya saphalaṃ tasya ceṣṭitam
paṅgavaste na sandeho janma teṣāṃ nirarthakam
ekāgramanasā yaistu na dṛṣṭo loṭaṇeśvaraḥ
piśācatvaṃ viyonitvaṃ na bhavettasya vai kule
saṅgame tatra yo gatvā snānaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi
puṇyaiścaiva tathā kuryād gītair nṛtyaiḥ prabodhanam
tataḥ prabhātāṃ rajanīṃ dṛṣṭvā natvā mahodadhim
āmantrya snānavidhinā snānaṃ tatra tu kārayet
oṃ namo viṣṇurūpāya tīrthanāthāya te namaḥ
sānnidhyaṃ kuru me deva samudra lavaṇāmbhasi
ityāmantraṇamantraḥ
agniśca tejo mṛḍayā ca deho reto 'dhā viṣṇuramṛtasya nābhiḥ
evaṃ bruvan pāṇḍava satyavākyaṃ tato 'vagāheta patiṃ nadīnām
iti snānamantraḥ
ājanmaśatasāhasraṃ yatpāpaṃ kṛtavān naraḥ
sakṛtsnānādvyapoheta pāpaughaṃ lavaṇāmbhasi
anyathā hi kuruśreṣṭha devayonirasau vibhuḥ
kuśāgreṇāpi vibudhairna spraṣṭavyo mahārṇavaḥ
sarvaratnapradhānastvaṃ sarvaratnākarākara
sarvāmarapradhāneśa gṛhāṇārghaṃ namo 'stu te
iti arvamantra
pitṛdevamanuṣyāṃśca saṃtarpya tadanantaram
uttīrya tīre tasyaiva pañcabhir dvijapuṃgavaiḥ
śrāddhaṃ samācaret paścāllokapālānurūpibhiḥ
kṛtvāgre lokapālāṃstu pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi
sampūjya ca yathānyāyaṃ tāneva brāhmaṇaiḥ saha
sukṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ paścāt tebhyaḥ sarvaṃ nivedayet
bālyātprabhṛti yatpāpaṃ kṛtaṃ vārdhakayauvane
prakhyāpayitvā tebhyo'gre lokapālān nimantrayet
bālyātprabhṛti yatkiṃcitkṛtam ā janmato 'śubham
viprebhyaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ tatsāṃnidhyaṃ sthiteṣu me
ityuktvā sa luṭhetpaścāttebhyo 'greṇa ca sammukham
anumānya ca tānpañca paścāt snānaṃ samācaret
śrāddhaṃ ca kāryaṃ vidhivatpitṛbhyo nṛpasattama
evaṃ kṛte nṛpaśreṣṭha sarvapāpakṣayo bhavet
jijñāsārthaṃ tu yaḥ kaścidātmānaṃ jñātum icchati
śubhāśubhaṃ ca yatkarma tasya niṣṭhāmimāṃ śṛṇu
snātvā tatra mahātīrthe luṭhamāno vrajennaraḥ
pāpakarmānyato yāti dharmakarmā vrajen nadīm
pāpakarmā tato jñātvā pāpaṃ me pūrvasaṃcitam
snātvā tīrthavare tasmindānaṃ dadyād yathāvidhi
loṭaṇeśvaram abhyarcya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
avakragamanaṃ gatvā mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena jñātvaivaṃ nṛpasattama
snātavyaṃ mānavaistatra yatra saṃnihito haraḥ
evaṃ snātvā vidhānena brāhmaṇān vedapāragān
pūjayetpṛthivīpāla sarvapāpopaśāntaye
evaṃ guṇaviśiṣṭaṃ hi tattīrthaṃ nṛpasattama
tasya tīrthasya māhātmyaṃ śṛṇuṣvaikamanā nṛpa
tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā saṃtarpya pitṛdevatāḥ
śrāddhaṃ yaḥ kurute tatra pitṝṇāṃ bhaktibhāvitaḥ
dānaṃ dadāti viprebhyo gobhūtilahiraṇyakam
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi koṭirvarṣaśatāni ca
vimānavaramārūḍhaḥ svargaloke mahīyate
narmadāsarvatīrthebhyaḥ snāne dāne ca yatphalam
tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti revāsāgarasaṅgame
suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ maṇimauktikabhūṣaṇam
govṛṣaṃ ca mahīṃ dhānyaṃ tatra dattvākṣayaṃ phalam
śubhasyāpyaśubhasyāpi tatra tīrthe na saṃśayaḥ
tatra tīrthe naraḥ kaścit prāṇatyāgaṃ yudhiṣṭhira
karoti bhaktyā vidhivattasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
koṭivarṣaṃ tu varṣāṇāṃ krīḍitvā śivamandire
vedavedāṅgavidvipro jāyate vimale kule
putrapautrasamṛddho 'sau dhanadhānyasamanvitaḥ
sarvavyādhivinirmukto jīvecca śaradāṃśatam
api dvādaśayātrāsu somanāthe yadarcite
kārttikyāṃ kṛttikāyoge tatpuṇyaṃ loṭaṇeśvare
gayā gaṅgā kurukṣetre naimiṣe puṣkare tathā
tatpuṇyaṃ labhate pārtha loṭaṇeśvaradarśanāt
yaḥ śṛṇoti naro bhaktyā paṭhyamānam idaṃ śubham
sarvapāpavinirmukto rudralokaṃ sa gacchati
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe loṭaṇeśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma viṃśatyuttaradviśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchettu rājendra revāyā dakṣiṇe taṭe
krośadvayāntare tīrthaṃ matṛtīrthād anuttamam
nāmnā haṃseśvaraṃ puṇyaṃ vaimanasyavināśanam
kaśyapasya kule jāto haṃso dākṣāyaṇīsutaḥ
brahmaṇo vāhanaṃ jātaḥ purā taptvā tapo mahat
saikadā vidhinirdeśaṃ vinā vaiyagryamāsthitaḥ
abhibhūtaḥ śivagaṇaiḥ praṇanāśa yudhiṣṭhira
dakṣayajñapramathane kāṃdiśīko vidhiṃ vinā
brahmaṇā saṃsṛto 'pyāśu nāyāti sa yadā khagaḥ
tadā taṃ śaptavānbrahmā pātayāmāsa vai padāt
tataḥ sa śaptamātmānaṃ matvā haṃsastvarānvitaḥ
pitāmahamupāgamya praṇipatyedam abravīt
haṃsa uvāca
tiryagyonisamutpannaṃ bhavāñchaptuṃ na cārhati
svabhāva eva tiryakṣu vivekavikalaṃ manaḥ
tathāpi deva pāpo 'smi yadahaṃ svāminaṃ tyaje
kiṃ tu dhāvadbhir atyugrairgaṇaiḥ śārvaiḥ pitāmaha
sahasāhaṃ bhayākrāntastrastastyaktvā palāyitaḥ
adyāpi bhayamevāhaṃ paśyannasmi vibho puraḥ
tena smṛto 'pi bhavatā nāvrajaṃ bhavadantike
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
iti bruvanneva hi dhāturagre haṃsaḥ śvasatyakṣipūjyaḥ sudīnaḥ
tiryañcaṃ māṃ pāpinaṃ mūḍhabuddhiṃ prabho puraḥ patitaṃ pāhi pāhi
eko devastvaṃ hi sargasya kartā nānāvidhaṃ sṛṣṭametattvayaiva
ahaṃ sṛṣṭastvīdṛśo yattvayā vai so 'yaṃ doṣo dhātar addhā tavaiva
śāpasya vānugrahasyāpi śaktastvatto nānyaḥ śaraṇaṃ kaṃ vrajāmi
sevādharmādvicyutaṃ dāsabhūtaṃ capeṭairhantavyaṃ vai tāta māṃ trāhi bhaktam
vidyāvidye tvatta evāvirāstāṃ dharmādharmau sadasad dyurniśe ca
nānābhāvāñjagatastvaṃ vidhatses taṃ tvāmekaṃ śaraṇaṃ vai prapadye
eko 'si bahurūpo 'si nānācitraikakarmataḥ
niṣkarmākhilakarmāsi tvāmataḥ śaraṇaṃ vraje
namonamo vareṇyāya varadāya namonamaḥ
namo dhātre vidhātre ca śaraṇyāya namonamaḥ
śikṣākṣaraviyukteyaṃ vāṇī me stauti kiṃ vibho
kā śaktiḥ kiṃ parijñānamidamuktaṃ kṣamasva me
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
evaṃ vadati haṃse vai brahmā prāha prasannadhīḥ
śikṣā dattā tavaiveyaṃ mā viṣādaṃ kṛthāḥ khaga
tapasā śodhayātmānaṃ yathā śāpāntamāpnuyāḥ
revāsevāṃ kuru snātvā sthāpayitvā maheśvaram
acireṇaiva kālena tataḥ saṃsthānamāpsyasi
yacceṣṭvā bahubhir yajñaiḥ samāptavaradakṣiṇaiḥ
gosvarṇakoṭidānaiśca tatphalaṃ sthāpite śive
brahmaghno vā surāpo vā svarṇahṛd gurutalpagaḥ
revātīre śivaṃ sthāpya mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ
tasmādbhargasarittīre sthāpayitvā triyambakam
viyuktaḥ sarvadoṣaistvaṃ yāsyase padamuttamam
evamuktaḥ sa vidhinā hṛṣṭatuṣṭaḥ khagottamaḥ
tathetyuktvā jagāmāśu narmadātīramuttamam
tapastaptvā kiyatkālaṃ sthāpayāmāsa śaṅkaram
svanāmnā bharataśreṣṭha haṃseśvaramanuttamam
pūjayitvā paraṃ sthānaṃ prāptavānkhagasattamaḥ
tatra haṃseśvare tīrthe gatvā snātvā yudhiṣṭhira
pūjayetparameśānaṃ sa pāpaiḥ parimucyate
stuvannekamanā devaṃ na dainyaṃ prāpnuyāt kvacit
śrāddhaṃ dīpapradānaṃ ca brāhmaṇānāṃ ca bhojanam
dattvā śaktyā nṛpaśreṣṭha svargaloke mahīyate
trikālam ekakālaṃ vā yo bhaktyā pūjayecchivam
navaprasūtāṃ dhenuṃ ca dattvā pārtha dvijottame
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi śivaloke mahīyate
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe haṃseśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikaviṃśadadhikadviśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tataḥ krośāntare gacchettilādaṃ tīrthamuttamam
tilaprāśanakṛdyatra jābāliḥ śuddhimāptavān
pitṛmātṛparityāgī bhrāturbhāryābhilāṣakṛt
putravikrayakṛtpāpaśchalakṛdguruṇā saha
evaṃ doṣasamāviṣṭo yatra yatrāpi gacchati
tatra tatrāpi dhikkāraṃ labhate satsu bhārata
na ko'pi saṃgatiṃ dhatte tena sārddhaṃ sabhāsvapi
iti lajjānvito vipraḥ kāle na mahatā nṛpa
cintāmavāpa mahatīm agatijño hi pāvane
cakāra sarvatīrthāni revāṃ cāpyavagāhayat
aṇivāpāntam āsādya dakṣiṇe narmadātaṭe
tasthau yatra vratī pārtha jābāliḥ prāśayaṃstilān
tilairekāśanaṃ kurvaṃs tathaivaikāntarāśanam
tryahaṣaḍdvādaśāhāśī pakṣamāsāśanastathā
kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādīni vratāni ca tilairapi
tilādatvamanuprāpto hyabdadvāsaptatiṃ kramāt
kālena gacchatā tasya prasanno 'bhavadīśvaraḥ
prādād ihāmutrikīṃ tu śuddhiṃ sālokyamātmakam
tena sa sthāpito devaḥ svanāmnā bharatarṣabha
tilādeśvarasaṃjñāṃ ca prāpa lokādapi prabhuḥ
tadā prabhṛti vikhyātaṃ tīrthaṃ pāpapraṇāśanam
tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu ca
upavāsaparaḥ pārtha tathaiva harivāsare
tilahomī tilodvartī tilasnāyī tilodakī
tiladātā ca bhoktā ca nānāpāpaiḥ pramucyate
tilairāpūrayelliṅgaṃ tilatailena dīpadaḥ
rudralokam avāpnoti punāty ā saptamaṃ kulam
tilapiṇḍapradānena śrāddhe nṛpatisattama
vikarmasthāśca gacchanti gatimiṣṭāṃ hi pūrvajāḥ
svargalokasthitāḥ śrāddhair brāhmaṇānāṃ ca bhojanaiḥ
akṣayāṃ tṛptimāsādya modante śāśvatīḥ samāḥ
pituḥ kulaṃ mātṛkulaṃ tathā bhāryākulaṃ nṛpa
kulatrayaṃ samuddhṛtya svargaṃ nayati vai naraḥ
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe tilādeśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma dvāviṃśadadhikadviśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tataḥ krośāntare pārtha vāsavaṃ tīrthamuttamam
vasubhiḥ sthāpitaṃ tatra sthitvā vai dvādaśābdakam
dharo dhruvaśca somaśca āpaścaivānilo 'nalaḥ
pratyūṣaśca prabhāsaśca vasavo 'ṣṭāvime purā
pitṛśāpaparikliṣṭā garbhavāsāya bhārata
nārmadaṃ tīrthamāsādya tapaścakruryatendriyāḥ
ārādhayantaḥ paramaṃ bhavānīpatim avyam
dvādaśābdāni rājendra tatastuṣṭo maheśvaraḥ
pratyakṣaḥ pradadau tebhyas tvabhīṣṭaṃ varamuttamam
tataḥ svanāmnā saṃsthāpya vasavastaṃ maheśvaram
jagmurākāśamāviśya prasanne sati śaṅkare
tataḥ prabhṛti vikhyātaṃ tīrthaṃ tadvāsavāhvayam
tasmiṃstīrthe mahārāja yo bhaktyā pūjayecchivam
yathālabdhopahāraiśca dīpaṃ dadyāt prayatnataḥ
śuklapakṣe tadāṣṭamyāṃ pratyahaṃ vāpi śaktitaḥ
aṣṭau varṣasahasrāṇi sa vasecchivasaṃnidhau
tataḥ śivālayaṃ yāti garbhavāsaṃ na paśyati
puṣpairvā pallavairvāpi phalairdhānyais tathāpi vā
pūjayeddevamīśānaṃ sa dainyaṃ nāpnuyāt kvacit
sarvaśokavinirmuktaḥ svargaloke mahīyate
ekāhamapi kaunteya yo vasedvāsaveśvare
pāparāśiṃ vinirdhūya bhānuvaddivi modate
viprāṃśca bhojayedbhaktyā dadyād vāsāṃsi dakṣiṇām
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe vāsaveśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma trayoviṃśatyadhikadviśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tataḥ krośāntare pārtha tīrthaṃ koṭīśvaraṃ param
yatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca japahomārcanādikam
bhaktyā kṛtaṃ naraistatra sarvaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet
tatra devāḥ sagandharvā ṛṣayaḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ
jaladhiṃ pratigacchanti narmadāṃ vīkṣituṃ kila
militāḥ koṭiśo rājanrevāsāgarasaṅgame
vinodamatulaṃ dṛṣṭvā revārṇavasamāgame
snātvā śivaṃ ca saṃsthāpya pūjayitvā maheśvaram
koṭīśvarābhidhānaṃ tu svasvabhaktyā vidhānataḥ
koṭītīrthe parāṃ siddhiṃ samprāptāḥ sarvatoṣaṇāt
tena tatpuṇyamatulaṃ sarvatīrtheṣu cottamam
tatra tīrthe tu yatkiṃcicchubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham
kriyate nṛpaśārdūla sarvaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet
tatra tīrthe tu mārgasthā ye kecidṛṣisattamāḥ
siddhāmṛtapadaṃ yānti pitṛlokaṃ tathottamam
uttare narmadātīre dakṣiṇe cāśritāśca ye
devalokaṃ gatās tatra iti me niścitā matiḥ
bilvārkapuṣpair dhattūrakuśakāśaprasūnakaiḥ
ṛtūdbhavaistathānyaiśca pūjayitvā maheśvaram
nānopacārair vidhivan mantrapūrvaṃ yudhiṣṭhira
dhūpadīpārdhanaivedyaistoṣayitvā ca dhūrjaṭim
śivalokamavāpnoti yāvadindrāścaturdaśa
pauṣakṛṣṇāṣṭamīyoge viśeṣaḥ pūjane smṛtaḥ
nityaṃ ca nṛpatiśreṣṭha caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu ca
śivamabhyarcya viprāṃśca bhojayed bhaktito varān
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe koṭīśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma caturviṃśatyadhikadviśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tataḥ krośāntare gacched alikātīrthamuttamam
alikā nāma gāndharvī kuśīlā kuṭilāśayā
citrasenasya dauhitrī vidyānandamṛṣiṃ gatā
vavre te svīkṛtā tena daśavarṣāṇi taṃ śritā
patiṃ jaghāna taṃ suptaṃ kasmiṃścit kāraṇāntare
gatvā nivedayāmāsa pitaraṃ ratnavallabham
pitrā mātrā ca saṃtyaktā bahubhirbhartsitā nṛpa
garbhaghnī tvaṃ patighnī tvamiti darśaya mā mukham
brahmaghnī yāhi pāpiṣṭhe parityaktā gṛhādvraja
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
iti duḥkhānvitā mūḍhā tābhyāṃ nirbhartsitā satī
tanuṃ tyaktuṃ manaścakre prāpya tīrthāntaraṃ kvacit
saṃpṛcchyamānā tīrthāni brāhmaṇebhyo yudhiṣṭhira
śrutvā pāpaharaṃ tīrthaṃ revāsāgarasaṅgame
tatra pārtha tapaścakre nirāhārā jitavratā
cāndrāyaṇairbrahmakūrcaiḥ karśayāmāsa vai tanum
evaṃ varṣaśataṃ sārddhaṃ vyatītaṃ tapasā nṛpa
tasyā viśuddhim icchantyāḥ śivadhyānārcanādibhiḥ
tataḥ katipayāhobhis tasyā jñātvā haṭhaṃ param
parituṣṭaḥ śivaḥ prāha pārvatyā paricoditaḥ
īśvara uvāca
putri mā sāhasaṃ kārṣīḥ śuddhadehāsi sāmpratam
tuṣṭo 'haṃ tapasā te 'dya varaṃ varaya vāñchitam
alikovāca
yadi tuṣṭo 'si deveśa varārhā yadyahaṃ matā
nānāpāpāgnitaptāyā dehi śuddhiṃ parāṃ mama
tvaṃ me nātho hyanāthāyāstvameva jagatāṃ guruḥ
dīnānāthasamuddhartā śaraṇyaḥ sarvadehinām
īśvara uvāca
tvaṃ bhadre śuddhadehāsi mā kiṃcid anuśocithāḥ
svanāmnā sthāpayitveha māṃ tataḥ svargameṣyasi
ityuktvā devadeveśastatraivāntaradhīyata
alikāpi tato bhaktyā snātvā saṃsthāpya śaṅkaram
dattvā dānaṃ ca viprebhyo lokamāpa mahotkaṭam
pitaraṃ ca samāsādya mātaraṃ ca yudhiṣṭhira
taiśca saṃmānitā prītyā bandhubhiḥ sālikā tataḥ
vimānavaramārūḍhā divyamālānvitā nṛpa
gaurīlokamanuprāptasakhitve 'dyāpi modate
tataḥ prabhṛti tatpārtha vikhyātam alikeśvaram
tatra tīrthe tu yā nārī puruṣo vā yudhiṣṭhira
snātvā sampūjayedbhaktyā mahādevamumāyutam
sa pāpairvividhairmukto lokamāpnoti śāṃkaram
mānasaṃ vācikaṃ pāpaṃ kāyikaṃ yatpurā kṛtam
sarvaṃ tadvilayaṃ yāti bhojayitvā dvijānsadā
dīpaṃ dattvā ca devāgre na rogaiḥ paribhūyate
dhūpapātraṃ vimānaṃ ca ghaṇṭāṃ kalaśameva ca
dattvā devāya rājendra śākraṃ lokamavāpnuyāt
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe revāsāgarasaṅgame 'likeśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma pañcaviṃśatyadhikadviśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tataḥ krośāntare puṇyaṃ tīrthaṃ tadvimaleśvaram
yatra snānena dānena japahomārcanādibhiḥ
vimaleśvaramārādhya yo yadicchetsa tallabhet
svargalābhādikaṃ vāpi pārthivaṃ vā yathepsitam
purā triśirasaṃ hatvā tvaṣṭuḥ putraṃ śatakratuḥ
yasya tīrthasya māhātmyādvaimalyaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ
yatra vedanidhirvipro mahattaptvā tapaḥ purā
nānākarmamalaiḥ kṣīṇair vimalo 'bhavad arkavat
mahādevaprasādena somavat priyadarśanaḥ
purā bhānumatīṃ bhānuḥ sutāṃ smaraśarārditaḥ
cakame tena doṣeṇa kuṣṭharogārdito 'bhavat
sa cāpyatra tapastaptvā vimalatvam upāgataḥ
mahādevena tuṣṭena svasthānaṃ mudito 'bhajat
tathaiva ca purā pārtha vibhāṇḍakasuto muniḥ
yogisaṅgaṃ vane prāpya pure ca nṛpates tathā
rājasaṃsargadoṣādvai mālinyaṃ paramātmanaḥ
vicārayannabhyupetya revāsāgarasaṅgamam
śāntayā bhāryayā sārddhaṃ taptvā dvādaśavatsarān
kṛcchracāndrāyaṇair devaṃ toṣayaṃstryambakaṃ muniḥ
mahādevena tuṣṭena so 'pi vaimalyamāptavān
śarvāṇyā preritaḥ śarvaḥ purā dāruvane nṛpa
mohanānmunipatnīnāṃ svaṃ dīkṣya vimalaṃ kila
vicārya paramasthānaṃ narmadodadhisaṅgamam
tatra sthitvā mahārāja tapastaptvā sahomayā
vimalo 'sau yato jātastenāsau vimaleśvaraḥ
tena nāmnā svayaṃ tasthau lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
tatastilottamāṃ sṛṣṭvā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
prajānātho 'pi tāṃ sṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvāgre sumanoharām
bhāviyogabalākrāntaḥ sa tasyāmabhiko 'bhavat
tena vīkṣya sadoṣatvaṃ revātīradvayaṃ śritaḥ
tīrthānyanusaranmaunī trisnāyī saṃsmarañchivam
revārṇavasamāyoge snātvā sampūjya śaṅkaram
kālenālpena rājarṣe brahmāpyamalatāṃ gataḥ
evamanye 'pi bahuśo devarṣinṛpasattamāḥ
tyaktvā doṣamalaṃ tatra vimalā bahavo 'bhavan
tathā tvamapi rājendra tatra snātvā śivārcanāt
amalo 'pi viśeṣeṇa vaimalyaṃ prāpsyase param
tatra snātvā naro nārī pūjayitvā maheśvaram
pāpadoṣavinirmukto brahmaloke mahīyate
tatropavāsaṃ yaḥ kṛtvā paśyeta vimaleśvaram
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ sarvaparvasu pārthiva
saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ hitvā yāti śivālayam
śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā vidhānena pitṝṇām anṛṇī bhavet
brāhmaṇān bhojayecchaktyā tebhyo dadyācca dakṣiṇām
yadyadiṣṭatamaṃ loke yaccaivātmahitaṃ gṛhe
tattadguṇavate deyaṃ tatraivākṣayamicchatā
svarṇadhānyāni vāsāṃsi chatropānatkamaṇḍalum
gṛhaṃ devasya vai śaktyā kṛtvā syād bhuvi bhūpatiḥ
gītanṛtyakathābhiśca toṣayet parameśvaram
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe vimaleśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaḍviṃśatyadhikadviśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
etāni tava saṃkṣepāt prādhānyāt kathitāni ca
na śakto vistarād vaktuṃ saṃkhyāṃ tīrtheṣu pāṇḍava
eṣā pavitrā vimalā nadī trailokyaviśrutā
narmadā saritāṃ śreṣṭhā mahādevasya vallabhā
manasā saṃsmared yastu narmadāṃ satataṃ nṛpa
cāndrāyaṇaśatasyāśu labhate phalamuttamam
aśraddadhānāḥ puruṣā nāstikāścātra ye sthitāḥ
patanti narake ghore prāhaivaṃ parameśvaraḥ
narmadāṃ sevate nityaṃ svayaṃ devo maheśvaraḥ
tena puṇyā nadī jñeyā brahmahatyāpahāriṇī
iyaṃ māheśvarī gaṅgā maheśvaratanūdbhavā
proktā dakṣiṇagaṅgeti bhāratasya yudhiṣṭhira
jāhnavī vaiṣṇavī gaṅgā brāhmī gaṅgā sarasvatī
iyaṃ māheśvarī gaṅgā revā nāstyatra saṃśayaḥ
yathā hi puruṣe devas traimūrtatvam upāśritaḥ
brahmaviṣṇumaheśākhyaṃ na bhedas tatra vai yathā
tathā sarittraye pārtha bhedaṃ manasi mā kṛthāḥ
koṭiśo hyatra tīrthāni lakṣaśaścāpi bhārata
tathā sahasraśo revātīradvayagatāni tu
vṛkṣāntarikṣasaṃsthāni jalasthalagatāni ca
kaḥ śaktastāni nirṇetuṃ vāgīśo vā maheśvaraḥ
smaraṇājjanmajanitaṃ darśanācca trijanmajam
saptajanmakṛtaṃ naśyet pāpaṃ revāvagāhanāt
devakāryaṃ kṛtaṃ tena agnayo vidhivaddhutāḥ
vedā adhītāścatvāro yena revāvagāhitā
prādhānyāccāpi saṃkṣepāt tīrthānyuktāni te mayā
na śakyo vistaraḥ pārtha śrotuṃ vaktuṃ ca vai mayā
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
vidhānaṃ ca yamāṃścaiva niyamāṃśca vadasva me
prāyaścittārthagamane ko vidhistaṃ vadasva me
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ mahārāja yacchreyaḥ pāralaukikam
śṛṇuṣvāvahito bhūtvā yathājñānaṃ vadāmi te
adhruveṇa śarīreṇa dhruvaṃ karma samācaret
avaśyameva yāsyanti prāṇāḥ prāghūrṇikā iva
dānaṃ vittādṛtaṃ vācaḥ kīrtidharmau tathā khyuṣaḥ
paropakaraṇaṃ kāyādasārātsāram uddharet
asminmahāmohamaye kaṭāhe sūryāgninā rātridivendhanena
māsartudarvīparighaṭṭanena bhūtāni kālaḥ pacatīti vārtā
jñātvā śāstravidhānoktaṃ karma kartum ihārhasi
nāyaṃ loko 'sti na paro na sukhaṃ saṃśayātmanaḥ
mantre tīrthe dvije deve daivajñe bheṣaje gurau
yādṛśī bhāvanā yasya siddhir bhavati tādṛśī
aśraddhayā hutaṃ dattaṃ tapastaptaṃ kṛtaṃ ca yat
asadityucyate pārtha na ca tatpretya no iha
yaḥ śāstravidhim utsṛjya vartate kāmakārataḥ
na sa siddhim avāpnoti na sukhaṃ na parāṃ gatim
santīha vividhopāyā nṛṇāṃ dehaviśodhanāḥ
tīrthasevāsamaṃ nāsti svaśarīrasya śodhanam
kṛcchracāndrāyaṇād yair vā dvitīyaṃ tīrthasevayā
yadā tīrthaṃ samuddiśya prayāti puruṣo nṛpa
tadā devāśca pitaras taṃ vrajantyanu khecarāḥ
paramā modapūrṇāste prayānty asyānuyāyinaḥ
kṛtvābhyudayikaṃ śrāddhaṃ samāpṛcchaya tu devatām
iṣṭabandhūṃśca viṣṇuṃ ca śaṅkaraṃ sagaṇeśvaram
vrajeddvijābhyanujñāto gṛhītvā niyamānapi
ekāśanaṃ brahmacaryaṃ bhūśayyāṃ satyavāditām
varjanaṃ ca parānnasya pratigrahavivarjanam
varjayitvā tathā drohavañcanādi nṛpottama
sādhuveṣaṃ samāsthāya vinayena vibhūṣitaḥ
dambhāhaṅkāramukto yaḥ sa tīrthaphalamaśnute
yasya hastau ca pādau ca manaścaiva susaṃyatam
vidyā tapaśca kīrtiśca sa tīrthaphalamaśnute
akrodhanaśca rājendra satyaśīlo dṛḍhavrataḥ
ātmopamaśca bhūteṣu sa tīrthaphalamaśnute
muṇḍanaṃ copavāsaśca sarvatīrtheṣvayaṃ vidhiḥ
varjayitvā kurukṣetraṃ viśālāṃ virajāṃ gayām
snānaṃ surārcanaṃ caiva śrāddhe vai piṇḍapātanam
viprāṇāṃ bhojanaṃ śaktyā sarvatīrtheṣvayaṃ vidhiḥ
prāyaścittanimittaṃ ca yo vrajedyatamānasaḥ
tasyāpi ca vidhiṃ vakṣye śṛṇu pārtha samāhitaḥ
ekāśanaṃ brahmacaryamakṣāralavaṇāśanam
snātvā tīrthābhigamanaṃ haviṣyaikānnabhojanam
varjayet patitālāpaṃ bahubhāṣaṇameva ca
parīvādaṃ parānnaṃ ca nīcasaṅgaṃ vivarjayet
vrajecca nirupānatko vasāno vāsasī śuciḥ
saṃkalpaṃ manasā kṛtvā brāhmaṇānujñayā vrajet
tīrthe gatvā tathā snātvā kṛtvā caiva surārcanam
duṣkarmato vimuktaḥ syād anutāpī bhaved yadi
vede tīrthe ca deve ca daivajñe cauṣadhe gurau
yādṛśī bhāvanā yasya siddhir bhavati tādṛśī
uktatīrthaphalānāṃ ca purāṇeṣu smṛtiṣvapi
arthavādabhavāṃ śaṅkāṃ vihāya bharatarṣabha
kṛtvā vicāraṃ śāstroktaṃ parikalpya yathocitam
kāyena kṛcchracaraṇe hyaśaktānāṃ viśuddhaye
jñātvā tīrthāviśeṣaṃ hi prāyaścittaṃ samācaret
tacchṛṇuṣva mahārāja narmadāyāṃ yathocitam
caturviṃśatisaṃkhyebhyo yojanebhyo vrajennaraḥ
caturviṃśatikṛcchrāṇāṃ phalamāpnoti śobhanam
ata ūrdhvaṃ yojaneṣu pādakṛcchram udāhṛtaḥ
tanmadhye ca mahārāja yo vrajecchuddhikāṅkṣayā
yojane yojane tasya prāyaścittaṃ vidurbudhāḥ
praṇavākhye mahārāja tathā revorisaṃgame
bhṛgukṣetre tathā gatvā phalaṃ taddviguṇaṃ smṛtam
saṅgame devanadyāśca śūlabhede nṛpottama
dviguṇaṃ pādahīnaṃ syāt karajāsaṃgame tathā
eraṇḍīsaṅgame tadvat kapilāyāśca saṃgame
kecit triguṇitaṃ prāhuḥ kubjārevotthasaṅgame
oṃkāre ca mahārāja tadapi syāt samañjasam
saṅgameṣu tathānyāsāṃ nadīnāṃ revayā saha
prāhuste sārdhakṛcchraṃ vai phalaṃ pūrvaṃ yudhiṣṭhira
triguṇaṃ kṛcchram āpnoti revāsāgarasaṅgame
kṛcchraṃ caturguṇaṃ proktaṃ śuklatīrthe yudhiṣṭhira
yojane yojane gatvā caturviṃśatiyojanam
tatra tatra vasedyastu suciraṃ nṛvarottama
revāsevāsamācāraḥ saṃyuktaḥ śuddhabuddhimān
dambhāhaṅkārarahitaḥ śuddhyarthaṃ sa vimucyate
iti te kathitaṃ pārtha prāyaścittārthalakṣaṇam
revāyātrāvidhānaṃ ca guhyametad yudhiṣṭhira
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
yojanasya pramāṇaṃ me vada tvaṃ munisattama
yajjñātvā niścitaṃ me syān manaḥśuddhestu kāraṇam
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu pāṇḍava vakṣyāmi pramāṇaṃ yojanasya yat
tathā yātrāviśeṣeṇa viśeṣaṃ kṛcchrasambhavam
tiryagyavodarāṇyaṣṭāvūrdhvā vā vrīhayastrayaḥ
pramāṇamaṅgulasyāhurvitastir dvādaśāṃgulā
vitastidvitayaṃ hastaścaturhastaṃ dhanuḥ smṛtam
sa eva daṇḍo gadito viśeṣajñair yudhiṣṭhira
dhanuḥsahasre dve krośaś catuḥkrośaṃ ca yojanam
etadyojanamānaṃ te kathitaṃ bharatarṣabha
yena yātrāṃ vrajan vetti phalamānaṃ nijārjitam
uktaṃ kṛcchraphalaṃ tīrthe jalarūpe nṛpottama
yathāviśeṣaṃ te vacmi pūrvokte tatra tatra ca
tanme śṛṇu mahīpāla śraddadhānāya kathyate
yasmiṃstīrthe hi yatproktaṃ phalaṃ kṛcchrādikaṃ nṛpa
tatrāpyupoṣaṇāt kṛcchraphalaṃ prāpnotyathādhikam
dinajāpyācca labhate phalaṃ kṛcchrasya śaktitaḥ
tatra vikhyātadeveśaṃ snātvā dṛṣṭvābhipūjya ca
praṇamya labhate pārtha phalaṃ kṛcchrabhavaṃ sudhīḥ
tīrthe mukhyaphalaṃ snānād dvitīyaṃ cāpyupoṣaṇāt
tṛtīyaṃ khyātadevasya darśanābhyarcanādibhiḥ
caturthaṃ jāpyayogena dehaśaktyā tvaharniśam
pañcamaṃ sarvatīrtheṣu kalpanīyaṃ hi dūrataḥ
tīrastho yojanādarvāgdaśāṃśaṃ labhate phalam
uktatīrthaphalātpārtha nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
upavāsena sahitaṃ mahānadyāṃ hi majjanam
apyarvāgyojanātpārtha dadyātkṛcchraphalaṃ nṛṇām
ṣaḍyojanavahā kulya nadyo 'lpā dvādaśaiva ca
caturviṃśatigā nadyo mahānadyas tato 'dhikāḥ
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe tīrthayātrādividhānaviśeṣakathanaṃ nāma saptaviṃśatyadhikadviśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
parārthaṃ tīrthayātrāyāṃ gacchataḥ kasya kiṃ phalam
kiyanmātraṃ muniśreṣṭha tanme brūhi kṛpānidhe
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
parārthaṃ gacchatastanme vadataḥ śṛṇu pārthiva
yathā yāvatphalaṃ tasya yātrādivihitaṃ bhavet
uttameneha varṇena dravyalobhādinā nṛpa
nādhamasya kvacit kāryaṃ tīrthayātrādisevanam
dharmakarma mahārāja svayaṃ vidvānsamācaret
śarīrasyāthavā śaktyā anyadvā kāryayogataḥ
dharmakarma sadā prāyaḥ savarṇenaiva kārayet
putrapautrādikairvāpi jñātibhir gotrasambhavaiḥ
śreṣṭhaṃ hi vihitaṃ prāhurdharmakarma yudhiṣṭhira
taireva kārayettasmānnottamairnādhamairapi
adhamena kṛtaṃ samyaṅ na bhavediti me matiḥ
uttamaścādhamārthe vai kurvandurgatimāpnuyāt
na śūdrāya matiṃ dadyānnocchiṣṭaṃ na haviṣkṛtam
na cāsyopadiśeddharmaṃ na cāsya vratamādiśet
japastapastīrthayātrā pravrajyā mantrasādhanam
devatārādhanaṃ dīkṣā strīśūdrapatanāni ṣaṭ
pativatnī patatyeva vidhavā sarvamācaret
sabhartṛkāśake patyau sarvaṃ kuryād anujñayā
gatvā parārthaṃ tīrthādau ṣoḍaśāṃśaphalaṃ labhet
gacchataśca prasaṅgena tīrthamarddhaphalaṃ smṛtam
anusaṅgena tīrthasya snāne snānaphalaṃ viduḥ
naiva yātrāphalaṃ tajjñāḥ śāstroktaṃ kalmaṣāpaham
pitrarthaṃ ca pitṛvyasya māturmātāmahasya ca
mātulasya tathā bhrātuḥ śvaśurasya sutasya ca
poṣakārthādayoścāpi mātāmahyā gurostathā
svasurmātṛṣvasuḥ paitryā ācāryādhyāpakasya ca
ityādyarthe naraḥ snātvā svayamaṣṭāṃśamāpnuyāt
sākṣātpitroḥ prakurvāṇaścaturthāṃśamavāpnuyāt
patipatnyormithaścārddhaṃ phalaṃ prāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ
bhāgineyasya śiṣyasya bhrātṛvyasya sutasya ca
ṣaṭtripañcacaturbhāgānphalamāpnoti vai naraḥ
iti te kathitaṃ pārtha pāramparyakramāgatam
kartavyaṃ jñātivargasya parārthe dharmasādhanam
varṣāṛtusamāyoge sarvā nadyo rajasvalāḥ
muktvā sarasvatīṃ gaṅgāṃ narmadāṃ yamunānadīm
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe parārthatīrthayātrāphalakathanaṃ nāmāṣṭaviṃśatyadhikadviśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
evaṃ te kathitaṃ rājanpurāṇaṃ dharmasaṃhitam
śivaprītyā yathā proktaṃ vāyunā devasaṃsadi
ṣaṣṭitīrthasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭikoṭistathaiva ca
ādimadhyāvasāneṣu narmadāyāṃ pade pade
mayā dvādaśasāhasrī saṃhitā yā śrutā purā
devadevasya gadataḥ sāmprataṃ kathitā tava
pṛṣṭastvayāhaṃ bhūpāla parvate 'marakaṇṭake
sthitaḥ saṃkṣepataḥ sarvaṃ mayā tatkathitaṃ tava
narmadācaritaṃ puṇyaṃ śṛṇu tasyāsti yatphalam
yatphalaṃ sarvavedaiḥ syāt saṣaḍaṅgapadakramaiḥ
paṭhitaiśca śrutair vāpi tasmād bahutaraṃ bhavet
satrayājī phalaṃ yatra labhate dvādaśābdikam
carite tu śrute devyā labhate tādṛśaṃ phalam
sarvatīrtheṣu yatpuṇyaṃ snātvā sāgaramāditaḥ
sakṛtsnātvā tathā śrutvā narmadāyāṃ phalaṃ hi tat
ādimadhyāvasānena narmadācaritaṃ śubham
yaḥ śṛṇoti naro bhaktyā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
sa prāpya śivasaṃsthānaṃ rudrakanyāsamāvṛtaḥ
rudrasyānucaro bhūtvā tenaiva saha modate
etad dharmamupākhyānaṃ sarvaśāstreṣu sattamam
deśe vā maṇḍale vāpi vā grāme nagare 'pi vā
gṛhe vā tiṣṭhate yasya cāturvarṇyasya bhārata
sa brahmā sa śivaḥ sākṣātsa ca devo janārdanaḥ
trividhaṃ kāraṇaṃ loke dharmapanthānamuttamam
devatānāṃ guruṃ śāstraṃ paramaṃ siddhikāraṇam
śrutveśvaramukhātpārtha mayāpi tava kīrtitam
dakṣiṇe cottare kūle yāni tīrthāni kānicit
pradhānataḥ supuṇyāni kathitāni viśeṣataḥ
sparśanād darśanāt teṣāṃ kīrtanācchravaṇāt tathā
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo rudralokaṃ sa gacchati
idaṃ yaḥ śṛṇuyān nityaṃ purāṇaṃ śivabhāṣitam
brāhmaṇo vedavidyāvān kṣatriyo vijayī bhavet
dhanabhāgī bhaved vaiśyaḥ śūdro vai dharmabhāgbhavet
saubhāgyaṃ santatiṃ svargaṃ nārī śrutvāpnuyāddhanam
brahmaghnaśca surāpaśca steyī ca gurutalpagaḥ
māhātmyaṃ narmadāyāstu śrutvā pāpabahiṣkṛtāḥ
pāpabhedī kṛtaghnaśca svāmiviśvāsaghātakaḥ
goghnaśca garadaścaiva kanyāvikrayakārakaḥ
ete śrutvaiva pāpebhyo mucyante nātra saṃśayaḥ
ye punarbhāvitātmānaḥ śṛṇvanti satataṃ nṛpa
pūjayanta idaṃ devāḥ pūjitā guravaśca taiḥ
narmadā pūjitā tena bhagavāṃśca maheśvaraḥ
tasmātsarvaprayatnena gandhapuṣpavibhūṣaṇaiḥ
pūjitaṃ parayā bhaktyā śāstrametatphalapradam
lekhāpayitvā sakalaṃ narmadācaritaṃ śubham
uttamaṃ sarvaśāstrebhyo yo dadāti dvijanmane
narmadāsarvatīrtheṣu snāne dāne ca yatphalam
tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti sa naro nātra saṃśayaḥ
etatpurāṇaṃ rudroktaṃ mahāpuṇyaphalapradam
svargadaṃ putradaṃ dhanyaṃ yaśasyaṃ kīrtivardhanam
sarvapāpaharaṃ pārtha duḥkhaduḥsvapnanāśanam
paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ rājan sarvakāmārthasiddhidam
śāntirastu śivaṃ cāstu lokāḥ santu nirāmayāḥ
gobrāhmaṇebhyaḥ svastyastu dharmaṃ dharmātmajāśrayaḥ
narakāntakarī revā satīrthā viśvapāvanī
narmadā dharmadā cāstu śarmadā pārtha te sadā
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe mārkaṇḍeyayudhiṣṭhirasaṃvāde revākhaṇḍapaṭhanaśravaṇadānādiphalaśrutivarṇanaṃ nāmaikonatriṃśadadhikadviśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīsūta uvāca
tathaiva tīrthastabakān vakṣye'ham ṛṣisattamāḥ
yaistu tīrthāvalīgumphaḥ pūrvoktairekataḥ kṛtaḥ
vibhakto bhaktalokānāmānandaprathanaḥ śubhaḥ
mṛkaṇḍatanayaḥ pūrvaṃ prāha pārthāya pṛcchate
yathā tathāhaṃ vakṣyāmi tīrthānāṃ stabakāniha
śivāmbupānajā puṇyā revā kalpalatā kila
tīradvayodbhūtatīrthaprasūnaiḥ puṣpitā śubhā
yatpuṇyagandhalakṣmyā vai trailokyaṃ surabhīkṛtam
tatpuṣpamakarandasya rasāsvādaviduttamaḥ
bhramaraḥ khalu mārkaṇḍo munirmatimatāṃ varaḥ
tatpuṣpamālāṃ hṛdaye tīrthastabakacitritām
dadhāti satataṃ puṇyāṃ munirbhṛgukulodvahaḥ
tasyāḥ stabakasaṃsthānaṃ vakṣye 'ham ṛṣisattamāḥ
oṅkāratīrthamārabhya yāvatpaścimasāgaram
saṃgamāḥ pañcatriṃśadvai nadīnāṃ pāpanāśanāḥ
daśaikamuttare tīre satriviṃśati dakṣiṇe
pañcatriṃśattamaḥ śreṣṭho revāsāgarasaṅgamaḥ
saṅgamaḥ sahitānyevaṃ revātīradvaye 'pi ca
catuḥśatāni tīrthāni prasiddhāni dvijottamāḥ
triśataṃ śivatīrthāni trayīstriṃśatsamanvitam
tatrāpi vyaktito vakṣye śṛṇudhvaṃ tāni sattamāḥ
mārkaṇḍeśvaratīrthāni daśa teṣu munīśvarāḥ
daśādityabhavānyatra navaiva kapileśvarāḥ
somasaṃsthāpitānyaṣṭau tāvanto narmadeśvarāḥ
koṭitīrthānyathāṣṭau ca sapta siddheśvarāstathā
nāgeśvarāśca saptaiva revātīradvaye 'pi tu
saptaiva vahnivihitānyathāpyāvartasaptakam
kedāreśvaratīrthāni pañca pañcendrajāni ca
varuṇeśāśca pañcaiva pañcaiva dhanadeśvarāḥ
devatīrthāni pañcaiva catvāro vai yameśvarāḥ
vaidyanāthāśca catvāraścatvāro vānareśvarāḥ
aṅgāreśvaratīrthāni tāvantyeva munīśvarāḥ
sārasvatāni catvāri catvāro dārukeśvarāḥ
gautameśvaratīrthāni trīṇi rāmeśvarāstrayaḥ
kapāleśvaratīrthāni trīṇi haṃsakṛtāni ca
trīṇyeva mokṣatīrthāni trayo vai vimaleśvarāḥ
sahasrayajñatīrthāni trīṇyeva munirabravīt
bhīmeśvarāstrayaḥ khyātāḥ svarṇatīrthāni trīṇi ca
dhautapāpadvayaṃ proktaṃ karañjeśadvayaṃ tathā
ṛṇamocanatīrthe dve tathā skandeśvaradvayam
daśāśvamedhatīrthe dve nandītīrthadvayaṃ dvijāḥ
manmatheśadvayaṃ caiva bhṛgutīrthadvayaṃ tathā
parāśareśvarau dvau ca ayonīsaṃbhavadvayam
vyāseśvaradvayaṃ proktaṃ pitṛtīrthadvayaṃ tathā
nandikeśvaratīrthe dve dvau ca gopeśvarau smṛtau
māruteśadvayaṃ tadvad dvau ca jvāleśvarau smṛtau
śuklatīrthadvayaṃ puṇyam apsareśadvayaṃ tathā
pippaleśvaratīrthe dve māṇḍavyeśvarasaṃjñite
dvīpeśvaradvayaṃ caiva prāha tadvadbhṛgūdvahaḥ
uttareśvaratīrthe dve aśokeśadvayī tathā
dve yodhanapure caiva rohiṇītīrthakadvayam
luṅkeśvaradvayaṃ khyātamākhyānaṃ muninā tathā
saikonaviṃśatiśataṃ tīrthānyekaikaśo dvijāḥ
stabakeṣu kṛtaṃ tīrthaṃ dviśataṃ sacaturdaśam
śaivānyetāni tīrthāni vaiṣṇavāni ca sattamāḥ
śṛṇudhvaṃ procyamānāni brāhmaśāktāni ca kramāt
aṣṭaviṃśatitīrthāni vaiṣṇavānyabravīnmuniḥ
teṣu vārāhatīrthāni ṣaḍeva munisattamāḥ
catvāri cakratīrthāni śeṣāṇyaṣṭādaśaiva hi
viṣṇunādhiṣṭhitāny eva prāha pūrvaṃ mṛkaṇḍajaḥ
tathaiva brahmaṇā siddhyai saptatīrthānyavīvadat
triṣu ca brahmaṇaḥ pūjā brahmeśāścaturo 'pare
aṣṭāviṃśanmayā khyātā yathāsaṅkhyaṃ yathākramam
etatpavitramatulaṃ hyetat pāpaharaṃ param
narmadācaritaṃ puṇyaṃ māhātmyaṃ munibhāṣitam
sūta uvāca
evamuddeśataḥ prokto revātīrthakramo mayā
yathā pārthāya saṃkṣepān mārkaṇḍo munirabravīt
avāntarāṇi tīrthāni teṣu guptānyanekaśaḥ
yatra yāvatpramāṇāni tānyākarṇayatānaghāḥ
oṅkāratīrthaparitaḥ parvatād amarakaṇṭāt
krośadvaye sarvadikṣu sārdhakoṭītrayī matā
tīrthānāṃ saṃkhyayā guptaprakaṭānāṃ dvijottamāḥ
koṭirekā tu tīrthānāṃ kapilāsaṅgame pṛthak
aśokavanikāyāśca tīrthaṃ lakṣaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
śatamaṃ gāragartāyāḥ saṅgame munisattamāḥ
tīrthānāmayutaṃ tadvatkubjāyāḥ saṅgame sthitam
śataṃ hiraṇyagarbhāyāḥ saṅgame samavasthitam
tīrthānāmaṣṭaṣaṣṭiśca viśokāsaṅgame sthitā
tathā sahasraṃ tīrthānāṃ saṃsthitaṃ vāgusaṅgame
śataṃ sarasvatīsaṅge śuklatīrthe śatadvayam
sahasraṃ viṣṇutīrtheṣu mahiṣmatyāmathāyutam
śūlabhede ca tīrthānāṃ sāgraṃ lakṣaṃ sthitaṃ dvijāḥ
devagrāme sahasraṃ ca tīrthānāṃ munirabravīt
luṅkeśvare ca tīrthānāṃ sāgrā saptaśatī sthitā
tīrthānyaṣṭottaraśataṃ maṇinadyāśca saṅgame
vaidyanāthe ca tīrthānāṃ śatamaṣṭādhikaṃ viduḥ
evaṃ tāvatpramāṇāni tīrthe kumbheśvare dvijāḥ
sāgraṃ lakṣaṃ ca tīrthānāṃ sthitaṃ revorasaṅgame
tataścāpyadhikāni syuriti mārkaṇḍabhāṣitam
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi vyāsadvīpāśritāni ca
saṅgame ca karañjāyāḥ sthitamaṣṭottarāyutam
eraṇḍīsaṅgame tadvattīrthānyaṣṭādhikaṃ śatam
dhūtapāpe ca tīrthānāṃ ṣaṣṭiraṣṭādhikā sthitā
skandatīrthe śataṃ puṇyaṃ tīrthānāṃ muniruktavān
kohaneśa ca tīrthānāṃ ṣaṣṭiraṣṭādhikā sthitā
sārdhakoṭī ca tīrthānāṃ sthitā vai korilāpure
rāmakeśavatīrthe ca sahasraṃ sāgramuktavān
asmāhake sahasraṃ ca tīrthāni nivasanti hi
lakṣāṣṭakaṃ sahasre dve śuklatīrthe dvijottamāḥ
tīrthāni kathayāmāsa purā pārthāya bhārgavaḥ
śatamaṣṭādhikaṃ prāha pratyekaṃ saṅgameṣu ca
nadīnāmavaśiṣṭānāṃ kāverīsaṅgamaṃ vinā
kāveryāḥ saṅgame viprāḥ sthitā pañcaśatī tathā
tīrthānāṃ parvasu tathā viśeṣo muninoditaḥ
mokṣatīrthaṃ hi satprāhuḥ purāṇapuruṣāśritam
bhṛgoḥ kṣetre ca tīrthānāṃ koṭirekā samāśritā
sādhikānāmṛṣiśreṣṭhā vaktuṃ śakto hi ko bhavet
sarvāmarāśrayaṃ proktaṃ sarvatīrthāśrayaṃ tathā
triṣu lokeṣu vikhyātaṃ pūjitaṃ siddhisādhanam
bhārabhūtyāṃ ca tīrthānāṃ sthitamaṣṭottaraṃ śatam
akrūreśvaratīrthe ca sārdhaṃ tīrthaśataṃ sthitam
vimaleśvaratīrthe tu revāsāgarasaṅgame
daśāyutāni tīrthānāṃ sādhikānyabravīnmuniḥ
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe tīrthasaṃkhyāparigaṇanavarṇanaṃ nāmaikatriṃśadadhikadviśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
iti vaḥ kathitaṃ viprā revāmāhātmyamuttamam
yathopadiṣṭaṃ pārthāya mārkaṇḍeyena vai purā
tathā tīrthakadambāśca teṣu tīrthaviśeṣataḥ
prādhānyena mayā khyātā yathāsaṅkhyaṃ yathākramam
etatpavitramatulaṃ hyetatpāpaharaṃ param
narmadācaritaṃ puṇyaṃ māhātmyaṃ munibhāṣitam
saptakalpānugo vipro narmadāyāṃ munīśvarāḥ
mṛkaṇḍatanayo dhīmānparamārthaviduttamaḥ
saṃsevya sarvatīrthāni nadīḥ sarvāśca vai purā
bahukalpasmarāṃ revāmālakṣya śivadehajām
me kaleti ca śarvoktāṃ śaraṇaṃ śarvajāṃ yayau
ajarāmamarāṃ devīṃ daityadhvaṃsakarīṃ parām
mahāvibhavasaṃyuktāṃ bhavaghnīṃ bhavajāhnavīm
tasyāmābadhya satprema jātaḥ so 'pyajarāmaraḥ
ṣaṣṭitīrthasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭikoṭyaśca sattamāḥ
vyavasthitāni revāyāstīrayugme pade pade
sāritaḥ paritaḥ santi satīrthāstu sahasraśaḥ
na tulāṃ yānti revāyāstāśca manye munīśvarāḥ
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ yatpṛṣṭamakhilaṃ dvijāḥ
yanmaheśamukhācchrutvā vāyurāha ṛṣīnprati
tadvanmṛkaṇḍatanayo 'pyanubhūyākhilāṃ nadīm
satīrthāṃ padaśaḥ prāha pāṇḍuputrāya pāvanīm
etacca kathitaṃ sarvaṃ saṃkṣepeṇa dvijottamāḥ
narmadācaritaṃ puṇyaṃ triṣu lokeṣu durlabham
kimanyaiḥ saritāṃ toyaiḥ sevitais tu sahasraśaḥ
yadi saṃsevyate toyaṃ revāyāḥ pāpanāśanam
mekalājalasaṃsevī muktimāpnoti śāśvatīm
yathā yathā bhajenmartyo yadyadicchati tīrthagaḥ
tattadāpnoti niyataṃ śraddhayāśraddhayāpi ca
idaṃ brahmā hariridamidaṃ sākṣātparo haraḥ
idaṃ brahma nirākāraṃ kaivalyaṃ narmadājalam
tāvadgarjanti tīrthāni nadyo hṛdayaphalapradāḥ
yāvanna smaryate revā sevāhevā kalau naraiḥ
dhruvaṃ loke hitārthāya śivena svaśarīrataḥ
śaktiḥ kāpi saridrūpā reveyamavatāritā
tāvadgarjanti yajñāśca vanakṣetrādayo bhṛśam
yāvanna narmadānāmakīrtanaṃ kriyate kalau
garimā gāṇyate tāvattapodānavratādiṣu
narairvā prāpyate yāvadbhuvi bhargabhavā dhunī
ye vasantyuttare kūle rudrasyānucarā hi te
vasanti yāmyatīre ye lokaṃ te yānti vaiṣṇavam
dhanyāste deśavaryāste yeṣu deśeṣu narmadā
narakāntakarī śaśvatsaṃśritā śarvanirmitā
kṛtapuṇyāśca te lokāḥ śokāya na bhavanti te
ye pibanti jalaṃ puṇyaṃ pārvatīpatisindhujam
idaṃ pavitramatulaṃ revāyāścaritaṃ dvijāḥ
śṛṇoti yaḥ kīrtayate mucyate sarvapātakaḥ
yatphalaṃ sarvavedaiśca saṣaḍaṅgapadakramaiḥ
śrutaiśca paṭhitaistasmātphalamaṣṭaguṇaṃ bhavet
satrayājī phalaṃ yacca labhate dvādaśābdikam
śrutvā sakṛcca revāyāścaritaṃ tatphalaṃ labhet
sarvatīrthāvagāhācca yatphalaṃ sāgarādiṣu
sakṛcchrutvā ca māhātmyaṃ revāyās tatphalaṃ labhet
etaddharmyamupākhyānaṃ sarvaśāstreṣvanuttamam
deśe vā maṇḍale vāpi nagare grāmamadhyataḥ
gṛhe vā tiṣṭhate yasya likhitaṃ sārvavārṇikam
sa brahmā sa śivaḥ sākṣātsa ca devo janārdanaḥ
dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ mārge 'yaṃ devasevitaḥ
gurūṇāṃ ca guruḥ śāstraṃ paramaṃ siddhikāraṇam
yaścedaṃ śṛṇuyānnityaṃ purāṇaṃ devabhāṣitam
brāhmaṇo vedavānbhūyātkṣatriyo vijayī bhavet
dhanāḍhyo jāyate vaiśyaḥ śūdro vai dharmabhāg bhavet
saubhāgyasantatiṃ nārī śrutvaitatsamavāpnuyāt
śriyaṃ saukhyaṃ svargavāsaṃ janma caivottame kule
rasabhedī kṛtaghnaśca svāmidhruṅ mitravañcakaḥ
goghnaśca garadaścaiva kanyāvikrayakārakaḥ
brahmaghnaśca surāpī ca steyī ca gurutalpagaḥ
narmadācaritaṃ śṛṇvaṃstāmabdaṃ yo 'bhiṣevate
sarvapāpavinirmukto jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
pākabhedī vṛthāpākī devabrāhmaṇanindakaḥ
parīvādī guroḥ pitroḥ sādhūnāṃ nṛpatestathā
te 'pi śrutvā ca pāpebhyo mucyante nātra saṃśayaḥ
ye punarbhāvitātmānaḥ śastraṃ śṛṇvanti nityaśaḥ
pūjayanti ca tacchāstraṃ nārmadaṃ vastrabhūṣaṇaiḥ
puṣpaiḥ phalaiś candanādyair bhojanair vividhair api
śāstre 'sminpūjite devāḥ pūjitā guravastathā
iha loke pare caiva nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
tasmātsarvaprayatnena gandhavastrādibhūṣaṇaiḥ
pūjayetparayā bhaktyā vācakaṃ śāstrameva ca
vedapāṭhaiśca yatpuṇyamagnihotraiśca pālitaiḥ
tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti narmadācarite śubhe
kurukṣetre ca yatpuṇyaṃ prabhāse puṣkare tathā
rudrāvarte gayāyāṃ ca vārāṇasyāṃ viśeṣataḥ
gaṅgādvāre prayāge ca gaṅgāsāgarasaṅgame
evamādiṣu tīrtheṣu yatpuṇyaṃ jāyate nṛṇām
narmadācaritaṃ śrutvā tatpuṇyaṃ sakalaṃ labhet
ādimadhyāvasāneṣu narmadācaritaṃ śubham
yaḥ śṛṇoti naro bhaktyā śṛṇudhvaṃ tatphalaṃ mahat
samāpya śivasaṃsthānaṃ devakanyāsamāvṛtaḥ
rudrasyānucaro bhūtvā śivena saha modate
dharmākhyānamidaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvākhyāneṣvanuttamam
gṛhe 'pi paṭhyate yasya caturvarṇasya sattamāḥ
dhanyaṃ tasya gṛhaṃ manye gṛhasthaṃ cāpi tatkulam
pustakaṃ pūjayedyastu narmadācaritasya tu
narmadā pūjitā tena bhagavāṃśca maheśvaraḥ
vācake pūjite tadvaddevāśca ṛṣayo 'rcitāḥ
lekhayitvā ca sakalaṃ revācaritamuttamam
bhūṣaṇaṃ sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ yo dadāti dvijanmane
narmadāsarvatīrtheṣu snānadānena yatphalam
tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti sa naro nātra saṃśayaḥ
etatpurāṇaṃ rudroktaṃ mahāpuṇyaphalapradam
svargadaṃ putradaṃ dhanyaṃ yaśasyaṃ kīrttivardhanam
dharmyamāyuṣyamatulaṃ duḥkhaduḥsvapnanāśanam
paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ cāpi sarvakāmārthasiddhidam
yatpradattamidaṃ puṇyaṃ purāṇaṃ vācyate dvijaiḥ
śivaloke sthitis tasya purāṇākṣaravatsarī
iti nigaditametannarmadāyāścaritraṃ pavanagaditamagryaṃ śarvavaktrādavāpya
tribhuvanajanavandyaṃ tvetadādau munīnāṃ kulapatipuratas tat sūtamukhyena sādhu
iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍasamāptirevākhaṇḍapustakadānādimāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma dvātriṃśadadhikadviśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
